    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

      $('rating_details').observe('prototip:shown', function() {
        if (this.up('#box')) {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: $('box').getStyle('z-index')})});
        } else {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });
      $('rating_details').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer11836935437264613362">The Shadowhunters of Los Angeles star in the first novel in Cassandra Clare’s newest series, The Dark Artifices, a sequel to the internationally bestselling Mortal Instruments series. <i>Lady Midnight</i> is a Shadowhunters novel.<br/><br/>It’s been five years since the events of <i>City of Heavenly Fire</i> that brought the Shadowhunters to the brink of oblivion.   <span id="freeText11836935437264613362" style="display:none">The Shadowhunters of Los Angeles star in the first novel in Cassandra Clare’s newest series, The Dark Artifices, a sequel to the internationally bestselling Mortal Instruments series. <i>Lady Midnight</i> is a Shadowhunters novel.<br /><br />It’s been five years since the events of <i>City of Heavenly Fire</i> that brought the Shadowhunters to the brink of oblivion. Emma Carstairs is no longer a child in mourning, but a young woman bent on discovering what killed her parents and avenging her losses.<br /><br />Together with her parabatai Julian Blackthorn, Emma must learn to trust her head and her heart as she investigates a demonic plot that stretches across Los Angeles, from the Sunset Strip to the enchanted sea that pounds the beaches of Santa Monica. If only her heart didn’t lead her in treacherous directions…<br /><br />Making things even more complicated, Julian’s brother Mark—who was captured by the faeries five years ago—has been returned as a bargaining chip. The faeries are desperate to find out who is murdering their kind—and they need the Shadowhunters’ help to do it. But time works differently in faerie, so Mark has barely aged and doesn’t recognize his family. Can he ever truly return to them? Will the faeries really allow it?<br /><br /> Glitz, glamours, and Shadowhunters abound in this heartrending opening to Cassandra Clare’s Dark Artifices series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11836935437264613362" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: $('box').getStyle('z-index')})});
        } else {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('edition_29762865').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('edition_29762865').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('edition_29762865').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

</script></div>

<div id="review_1154836302" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1154836302" />
    <a title="Emma Giordano" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30604861-emma-giordano"><img alt="Emma Giordano" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1569693958p2/30604861.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1154836302?book_show_action=true">Jan 03, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emma Giordano" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emma Giordano" href="/user/show/30604861-emma-giordano">Emma Giordano</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1154836302" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12649147609471943152">OH MY GOODNESS. I don't think I'll ever be able to say it's better than The Mortal Instruments . . . but WOWWWW WAS THIS BOOK ABSOLUTELY AMAZING!<br/><br/>This book was absolutely phenomenal. I think it is some of Cassandra Clare's best work to date. To the people who say all of Cassie's books are the same, I hope Lady Midnight finally shuts you up. No more stories about "orphaned girls who aren't aware of their supernatural powers." (P.S. Clary was never an orphan so I don't know why I keep seeing that a</span>
  <span id="freeText12649147609471943152" style="display:none">OH MY GOODNESS. I don't think I'll ever be able to say it's better than The Mortal Instruments . . . but WOWWWW WAS THIS BOOK ABSOLUTELY AMAZING!<br /><br />This book was absolutely phenomenal. I think it is some of Cassandra Clare's best work to date. To the people who say all of Cassie's books are the same, I hope Lady Midnight finally shuts you up. No more stories about "orphaned girls who aren't aware of their supernatural powers." (P.S. Clary was never an orphan so I don't know why I keep seeing that associated with TMI?) It was so wonderful to jump into the Shadow world from a perspective we've never seen before. Here's a girl who's been a Shadowhunter all her life, who grew up with all of the customs we're so used to learning about throughout the past books, who's already lived through a war and survived. Even though it's the same world, it is so unbelievably different from anything I've read from Cassie before. Given, some of that may have to do with the fact that this is the first totally new and full novel I've read from Cassie Clare in 2014, but I do believe most of it is attributed to the fact that she's grown as a writer and story teller.<br /><br />From page one of this book, I can already sense a level of sophistication and improvement in her writing. There's an unfamiliar level of seriousness I haven't seen in the Shadow World before. It's intense, it's insane, and it's REAL. The characters in this book seem way more grounded than our beloved TMI/TID cast. I think some of that may have to do with the fact that there aren't jokes 24/7 (thought the comedy in this book is A+!) but each character is extremely individual and realistic in my opinion. I love absolutely all of them. It was so strange to start a book knowing quite a bit about this group of characters before starting; That's a TOTALLY new experience for me.<br /><br />I will say, this story was a bit slow to start. The first 100-200 pages were kind of slow, but I think it was more just getting used to a new world with new characters and a new story. As soon as the book picked up, I couldn't put it down! From there on, this book is a non stop thriller with everything you could possibly want from a new installment of the Shadowhunter Chronicles.<br /><br />Lady Midnight has taken the Shadow World further than I've ever imagined. I can't remember ever having so many theories for a series, and I am just EXPLODING with all of the new information that's revealed to us. I'm halfway through the book, thinking to myself, "I need Queen of Air and Darkness NOW because I cannot wait until 2018 to know the truth!" This story went in so many directions I wasn't expecting at the start, and I'm dying to see how things play out in the rest of the trilogy.<br /><br />That being said you DEFINITELY need to read all of Cassandra Clare's works prior to this because we get ALL THE TMI AND TID FEELS. If there's one thing I love about Cassie's books, it's the way she's able to throw in references of our favorite characters so subtly and endlessly give us the satisfaction we desire from her previous books. But that means for those of you who aren't totally caught up yet, STAY AWAY BECAUSE THE SPOILERS ARE EVERYWHERE.<br /><br />All in all, this book was absolutely fantastic. I never realized how much I wanted from this book, and Cassie managed to fulfill all of those unconscious desires I had for the future of this world. I can't remember the last time I loved a first book in a series this much. If that review hasn't sold you, I hit page 668 and turned DIRECTLY to page one to start all over again. Lady Midnight was absolutely phenomenal. I'm so proud of Cassie for never failing to disappoint me, always being an insanely talented writer, and continuing on with a world I know is so dear to her heart. I hope you all absolutely adore Lady Midnight as I did, and I cannot wait to post the spoiler-filled discussion I have prepared for my YouTube channel: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.youtube.com/user/emmmabooks">https://www.youtube.com/user/emmmabooks</a>. Happy reading my fellow Shadowhunters &lt;3<br /><br />*Disclaimer- I was sent an advanced copy of this book by Simon &amp; Schuster in exchange for an honest review. All opinions included in this review as well as my future video are entirely my own.*</span>
  <a data-text-id="12649147609471943152" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer1586200228638732530">THIS FIRST PART WAS ORIGINALLY WRITTEN IN 2012.<br/>Jesus the book isn't even out yet and you guys are trashing it already. Seriously, wait at least until it comes out, read it and THEN give your opinion. Right now it's just useless and pissing all of us fans off. She's not milking this. If she really just wanted more money, she wouldn't work so hard on all of this beautiful material she's creating for US. FOR US.   <span id="freeText1586200228638732530" style="display:none">THIS FIRST PART WAS ORIGINALLY WRITTEN IN 2012.<br />Jesus the book isn't even out yet and you guys are trashing it already. Seriously, wait at least until it comes out, read it and THEN give your opinion. Right now it's just useless and pissing all of us fans off. She's not milking this. If she really just wanted more money, she wouldn't work so hard on all of this beautiful material she's creating for US. FOR US. She doesn't have to do this, she could be working as a doctor or a lawyer and making money. And if you think those two jobs are harder and that writing is easier, you're 100% wrong. It's not easy, it's hard as hell but she does it. AND SHE DOES IT BEAUTIFULLY. It's even harder to get published and get enough books sold. Do your research before you go around calling people cash cows. We've all got to make a living. Some people do it by working at jobs that they absolutely hate and some, like Ms. Clare, do it by sticking with what they're passionate about. So what if she makes money? Her books are amazing and if you don't like them, that's fine. But it's rude to trash talk a series that isn't even written yet. In fact, it's rude to trash talk anything but the least you could do is hold off until you have something TO trash talk.<br /><br />----<br /><br />OH MY GOD. I knew this book would be amazing and it WAS. SO. FREAKING. AMAZING.<br /><br />Cassandra Clare, you have done it yet again. You've managed to make me care so much about characters I just met and made me feel their happiness, pain, sadness as if it were my own. I was so sad when I saw the last page. And then The Last Conversation... really? REALLY?! Gah!<br /><br />I really hope that the people who were trash talking have read it and been stunned. She created yet another beautiful masterpiece and I was more than happy to spend money on it.<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8081333513506806505">Update After 2017 Reread:<br/>I still absolutely love this first book! It is a solid start to what is most likely going to be an amazing series. However, I disagree with former me's review (down below). I think I was still high on the adrenaline of the finale while reading that, because, personally, it is not better than Clockwork Princess. I mean, that was a <i>very</i> bold statement. What was I thinking? It's amazing, but nothing can come to Clockwork Princess (not yet).<br/><br/>Original Review:<br/>My favorite Cassan</span>
  <span id="freeText8081333513506806505" style="display:none">Update After 2017 Reread:<br />I still absolutely love this first book! It is a solid start to what is most likely going to be an amazing series. However, I disagree with former me's review (down below). I think I was still high on the adrenaline of the finale while reading that, because, personally, it is not better than Clockwork Princess. I mean, that was a <i>very</i> bold statement. What was I thinking? It's amazing, but nothing can come to Clockwork Princess (not yet).<br /><br />Original Review:<br />My favorite Cassandra Clare book so far, <i>including</i> Clockwork Princess. I KNOW.<br />It wasn't just a war between the good guys vs. the evil villain, but was an action-packed mystery filled with family, friends, magic, murder, and forbidden love. WOWZA!<br />I loved how different every character felt. Especially how Ty, Mark, and Arthur had complex and different ways of thinking and dealing with issues. I'm so happy that Cassandra Clare wrote about mental illnesses in the Shadowhunter community and why we haven't really seen it so far in any of her other books. I also am happy that Julian, the love interest, wasn't like all of the other love interests that we've seen so far in her books: jokey and sarcastic. Julian was much more mature than the others because of circumstances beyond his control and seemed much more grounded. The way he took care of the kids *SWOON*. He's definitely my second favorite of the Cassandra Clare men so far (Will Herondale will never be usurped let's be honest.)<br /><br />There's so much left that I want to talk about, but I'm going to leave those things for my video review, which will come soon to my channel!</span>

    <a title="Melanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie"><img alt="Melanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577914102p2/3030788.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2570227019?book_show_action=true">Oct 22, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie">Melanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=demons">demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=quarantine-reads">quarantine-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=fae">fae</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=read-in-2020">read-in-2020</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2570227019" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11294889045950789208"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1541889883i/26575718._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>1.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2008644944' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Bones</a> ★★★<br/>2.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2373838717' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Ashes</a> ★★<br/>3.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2463489480' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Glass</a> ★★★<br/>1.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2465856942' rel='nofollow noopener'>Clockwork Angel</a> ★★★<br/>4.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2489169365' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Fallen Angels</a> ★<br/>2.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2518308849' rel='nofollow noopener'>Clockwork Prince</a> ★★★★<br/>5.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2526157370' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Lost Souls</a> ★★★★<br/>3.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2531117647' rel='nofollow noopener'>Clockwork Princess</a> ★★★★★<br/>6.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2544728646' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Heavenly Fire</a> ★★★★★<br/>*.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2552335362' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Bane Chronicles</a> ★★★<br/>*.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2564114842' rel='nofollow noopener'>Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy</a> ★★★<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“No one is ever the villain of their own story.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><i>Lady Midnight</i> was completely worth me reading eleven back-list Cassie Clare titles for. Holy shit, this book was everything. Everything. And honest</span>
  <span id="freeText11294889045950789208" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1541889883i/26575718._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2008644944" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Bones</a> ★★★<br>2.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2373838717" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Ashes</a> ★★<br>3.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2463489480" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Glass</a> ★★★<br>1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2465856942" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Angel</a> ★★★<br>4.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2489169365" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Fallen Angels</a> ★<br>2.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2518308849" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Prince</a> ★★★★<br>5.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2526157370" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Lost Souls</a> ★★★★<br>3.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2531117647" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Princess</a> ★★★★★<br>6.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2544728646" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Heavenly Fire</a> ★★★★★<br>*.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2552335362" rel="nofollow noopener">The Bane Chronicles</a> ★★★<br>*.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2564114842" rel="nofollow noopener">Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy</a> ★★★<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“No one is ever the villain of their own story.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><i>Lady Midnight</i> was completely worth me reading eleven back-list Cassie Clare titles for. Holy shit, this book was everything. Everything. And honestly this was one of the best things I’ve read all year. I am so in love, friends. This world just gets more complex, the banter gets funnier, the cast gets more diverse, and the stories get more and more enthralling. And this is easily the best book I’ve read from Cassie Clare yet. <br><br>But I went into this brand-new series, that has been building up in the previous series for some time now, never expecting the main story to be about a secret murderous cult. Like, the blessings. Basically, in <i>Lady Midnight</i> Emma is still unable to let the mysterious deaths of her parents go unsolved, even though everyone else thinks they were just the first casualties of the start of the Dark War. But it has been five years since then, and the Cold Peace is still being held up by the Shadowhunters, making it so no one can help or work with the fae. <br><br>Emma and the Blackthorns are living back at the LA Institute, and upholding that law even though they know it’s wrong. That is, until they get an offer that they can’t refuse. And we are thrown into a world of ley lines, sacrificial killings, necromancer magic, and a baffling puzzle that Emma and the gang need to figure out quickly. <br><br><i>Lady Midnight</i> is truly a book all about forbidden love. It is filled with angst, heartbreak, and pain. But it is so expertly done, that you’ll ask for more and say please while doing so. Cassandra Clare is just perfecting her writing, her stories, her characters, her plot twists, and her diversity with every single book. This book honestly blew me away. Also, yes, you need to read all eleven books leading up to his one, truly. <br><br><b>Please use caution reading the rest of this review if you have not read this book and all the series leading up to this book!</b> And as always, I’m going to do a little mini character breakdown on my thoughts and feelings on all the main characters in this book. <b>Spoilers ahead!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1541888709i/26575652._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(Perfect art by <a href="http://loweana.tumblr.com/post/143271336958/emmacarstajrs-black-hana-she-didnt-know" rel="nofollow noopener">Loweana</a> - who seriously makes my favorite art for every single fandom; <i>The Cruel Prince</i>, <i>Six of Crows</i>, and now <i>The Dark Artifices</i>!)<br><br>➽ <b>Emma Carstairs</b> - My queen, my love, my entire heart. My favorite main character in… forever. I’m not joking, I actually like her that much. Easily my favorite character in all of Cassie Clare’s books. Wow, The blessings. I’m not deserving. <br><br>➽ <b>Julian Blackthorn</b> - My soft, sweet boy. Too pure for this world and all the Shadowhunters. I will protect him at all costs. Also, full disclosure, I’ve had a thing for the “dark haired, broody, tortured artist” type since high school and Adrian from <i>Vampire Academy</i> and Julian really is the epitome of that, too. And some of his one-liners? God, I was swooning so hard. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“These pictures are my heart. And if my heart was a canvas, every square inch of it would be painted over with you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>➽ <b>Mark Blackthorn</b> - Mark Blackthorn is responsible for 90% of the angst I felt in this book. “Why lie?” is now my favorite ending line of every book and I will be haunted. Also, what a bi icon. My heart. <br><br>➽ <b>Kieran</b> - My dude really messed up in the middle of this book, but my subconscious just falls in love with all the queer faeries Seriously, it is beyond my control at this point. Plus, you all know that fae princes are literally my greatest weakness in this life, so….<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You are all that exists on the earth and under the sky that I do love.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>➽ <b>Cristina Rosales</b> - What an amazing new character. Cristina is Latinx and from Mexico and the most precious angel in the world. Her and Emma’s friendship was so wonderful and just warmed my heart during every scene. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1541888709i/26575654._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(Gorgeous art by <a href="http://hauntedduckprincess.tumblr.com/post/141892435486/not-sure-if-i-like-it-but-still-from-the-all" rel="nofollow noopener">Haunted Duck Princess</a>!)<br><br>➽ <b>Livvy Blackthorn</b> - This sweet little protector. I love Livvy so much, but I’m so scared how she is going to handle possibly being alone. <br><br>➽ <b>Tiberius Blackthorn</b> - Ty is honestly one of the best characters I’ve read about in years. Cassie Clare has done such a beautiful job with his character and showing that people on the Autism spectrum just learn and consume information differently; never wrongly. But I don’t want him and Livvy to separate, I’m weak. <br><br>➽ <b>Dru Blackthorn</b> - This shy little sweetheart gave me so many feels in this book. And again, I think Cassie Clare creating a thirteen-year-old struggling with body image is something I wish I had when I was thirteen. Every book, every series, every new character, Cassie just impresses me more and more. And I can’t wait to see more of Drusilla. <br><br>➽ <b>Octavian Blackthorn</b> - My heart always breaks for Tavvy, because even though he is only seven, all he has ever known is war. I mean, that’s so relatable to our world, and that breaks my heart, too. <br><br>➽ <b>Diego Rocío Rosales</b> - I honestly really like Diego, who is also Latinx and followed Cristina from Mexico, but I don’t want him to ruin my polyamorous dreams, but if he’s willing to add to them then I will be the happiest human on Earth. Thanks. But I am really scared to meet Jaime. <br><br>➽ <b>Gwyn</b> - Leader of the Hunt and stealer of my heart. Give me everything about this man, because I am highkey ready to call him daddy. <br><br>➽ <b>Iarlath</b> - Someone kill this man, quick. <br><br>➽ <b>Anselm Nightshade</b> - Vampire and pizza place owner! That combination is going to lead to nothing good. <br><br>➽ <b>Arthur Blackthorn</b> - I lowkey dislike Arthur. I know he has been though SOME SHIT, but I just feel so damn bad for Julian every time I think of him, and it just really ruins his character for me. <br><br>➽ <b>Johnny Rook</b> - This death was hella brutal. I was not prepared. But I will also say that I was so surprised when this book started out, on page one, with the Shadow Market and introduced us to this character, because I know the short stories that are currently being published are all about this magical place and I can’t wait to learn more. <br><br>➽ <b>Kit Rook</b> - AKA: Christopher Herondale. DAMN! I honestly screamed at this reveal. I can’t wait to learn everything about him. Also, this really solidifies that you really should read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2564114842" rel="nofollow noopener">Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy</a> before starting this book. <br><br>➽ <b>Diana Wrayburn</b> - Questionable face tat, but I can’t wait to learn more about her. <br><br>➽ <b>Malcolm Fade</b> - If <i>Lady Midnight</i> taught me anything, it is that warlocks are so damn over-powered. Holy moly, the power this dude had. Also, friendly reminder: no body = no death. Okay, thanks, bye. <br><br>➽ <b>Annabel</b> - Oh shit. Apparently the 2 AM "u up?" text is powerful. I’m scared, friends. <br><br>➽ <b>Tessa &amp; Jem</b> - That “item” that they were after. Shit, son. But seeing Jem build a relationship with Emma? So beautiful, I don’t even have words for it. I really hope that they are in <i>Lord of Shadows</i> more, because I honestly can’t get enough of them. <br><br>➽ <b>Clary &amp; Jace</b> - Holy shit, mom and dad are running the NY Institute now? Damn, they grow up fast. Real talk, one of my favorite moments of this book was Jace and Mark’s heart to heart, where he tells him that he has only given witchlight to two people before. Ahhh, the feels. <br><br>➽ <b>Izzy &amp; Simon</b> - Um, how are my babies engaged?!?! Ahhhhh! I honestly screamed when this information was presented, even though we didn’t get to see my favorites in this book at all. But still, I am so damn happy, and they deserve the world, and each other, and I’m honestly just overcome with emotions. <br><br>And you all knew I wasn’t going to write this long review and not talk more about the budding polyamorous relationship that I think Cassie Clare is building for us. I truly think with my entire body and soul that Cassie Clare wanted to have Tessa, Jem, and Will be in a polyamorous relationship, but it was still not that talked about back when <i>The Internal Devices</i> came out. But, dear reader, I think she is going to right her wrongs and give us the relationship of my dreams. And with two of the partners being fae? Lord, this is my actual dreams. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It was a sort of love few other people could understand. It was total and it was overwhelming and it could be cruel.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>But I know that Emma and Julian’s forbidden relationship is going to be the actual death of me. The only really negative thing I can say about this book is that I think the laws revolving around parabatai and the age restrictions that make these kids pick lifelong and life-altering relationships is so unbelievable. And let’s be real, Emma and Julian got done so dirty by their forced arrangement. But seeing how this bond is going to… maybe ruin them? Lord, I can’t. I actually can’t. And Mark Blackthorn is just going to intensify the angst, but I’m highkey ready for that!<br><br>I always appreciate that the heart of every Shadowhunter novel is about oppression and prejudices that impact everyone; friends, families, entire societies. The Clave is the political force that makes and implements the rules in this world, and much like my own world, many are really harmful, extremely backwards, and very exclusionary. And I love seeing young people fight back against the generation that wants to keep them in these broken cycles that are filled with hate and fear.<br><br>Another cool addition that this book gave us was the talk of Scholomance. I feel like I don’t remember this being something in the other books, and it is like a detective school, but Shadowhunter style. Diego already attended it, and it looks like Ty is going to eventually go to it, and I’m just really interested to see more. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“There is nothing more important than love. And no law higher.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Okay, let’s talk about the sex. First off, birth control runes? Praise/bless. I loved this more than words and Clary is honest to god doing the lord’s work. The sex on the beach. Like, it might be a tiny bit unrealistic (sand is not your friend during sex, I promise) but like, I had to wait 102 books for Jace to whip out that condom in Hell, but Cassie Clare gives us a hot sex scene in this first book of a series? The blessings. And Julian was the virgin and not Emma? The gifts keep on coming. Seriously, you all, I was screaming with joy over everything in chapter eighteen. Also, huge shout out to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/69919640-sol-thebookishking" rel="nofollow noopener">Solly</a> for sending me <a href="http://cassandraclare.tumblr.com/post/141990964319/as-promised-cassandra-jeans-emma-and-jules-from" rel="nofollow noopener">the naughty version of the beach scene</a>, because he knows me.<br><br>Also, a big shout out to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7285286-nana" rel="nofollow noopener">Lea</a> for sending me <a href="http://asstroashton.tumblr.com/post/141018497405/a-long-conversation-the-dark-artifices/amp" rel="nofollow noopener">the short story that is only found in first editions of <i>Lady Midnight</i></a>! And, friends, it was perfection! Overall, this is one of the best things I’ve read all year and I am so damn thankful that I read all those other books to get to this one. I experienced pure happiness while reading this book, from the first to last page. And I am literally posting this review and running back to my bookshelves to pick up <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2589314651" rel="nofollow noopener">Lord of Shadows</a>!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I breathe when you breathe, I bleed when you bleed, I’m yours and you’re mine, you’ve always been mine, and I have always, always belonged to you!”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1541888709i/26575653._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(Beautiful art by <a href="https://twitter.com/CassandraJP?ref_src=twsrc%5Egoogle%7Ctwcamp%5Eserp%7Ctwgr%5Eauthor" rel="nofollow noopener">Cassandra Jean</a>!)<br><br><a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://open.spotify.com/user/meltotheany?si=kHJ5JnLHQsSp23fDe0qxSQ" rel="nofollow noopener">Spotify</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a><br><br><b>Content and trigger warnings</b> for murder, death, loss of a loved one, torture, blood depictions, self-harm, anxiety attacks, PTSD, talk of cancer, and graphic violence.<br><br>I read this for the <a href="https://youtu.be/g_bDsdsIIXQ" rel="nofollow noopener">Stay Home Reading Rush</a> &amp; <a href="https://youtu.be/hcCi_PoUBX8" rel="nofollow noopener">OWLs Magical Readathon 2020</a>! ⚡</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1061093561" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16747359216084856980">It took me three weeks to finish this book. THREE! <br/><br/>But that doesn't mean I didn't like it (on the contrary), it was just because this was a really eventful month and it messed up my reading schedule badly, for two weeks I read only one chapter per day, so now you see why it took me so long to finish it. BUT I FINALLY DID. AND NOW I WANT/NEED MORE.<br/><br/>I mean... my interest wasn't really picked until page 350 or so... but after that page everything was full of gasps and squeals and cries of rage and/o</span>
  <span id="freeText16747359216084856980" style="display:none">It took me three weeks to finish this book. THREE! <br><br>But that doesn't mean I didn't like it (on the contrary), it was just because this was a really eventful month and it messed up my reading schedule badly, for two weeks I read only one chapter per day, so now you see why it took me so long to finish it. BUT I FINALLY DID. AND NOW I WANT/NEED MORE.<br><br>I mean... my interest wasn't really picked until page 350 or so... but after that page everything was full of gasps and squeals and cries of rage and/or happiness. I'm not going to do a full review here, maybe I'll make a full discussion in my channel, but here I'll just say a few important points:<br><br>- I LOVE THE BLACKTHORN KIDS. EVERYONE. They are so precious, and not only that, they are a really interesting mix of characters! Definitely Mark, Ty, Livvy, Dru, Tavvy and Julian (SPECIALLY JULIAN) now have a spot in my heart.<br><br>- So, Julian, I love him, but not in the "book boyfriend" way, is more like he's my son and I have to protect him from the evils of this world. The thing is... he doesn't really need protection! He really surprised me throughout the book! He is REALLY ruthless, and I wasn't expecting it! The fact that he's capable to do ANYTHING to make things go his way and to protect his family is admirable, but also a little unsettling. I love that about him. And I love that he's passionate and caring and... just a really interesting and well-built character! <br><br>- I also like Emma, and Cristina, and Perfect Diego. I also like Kieran. Cassandra Clare really knows how to create great characters!<br><br>- I obviously ship Emma and Julian (and I'm rooting for them), but OMG, the whole thing that happened at the end left me RAGING. I think the reason why parabatai love is forbidden is believable, but I didn't like the way Emma handled the situation. I was like: REALLY, REALLY??? THAT HAPPENS IN EVERY BOOK EVER. I mean, I understand why she did what she did, but we already know the mess that <i>that</i> will cause. <br><br>- I shouted out loud when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[THEY REVEALED THAT KIT WAS A HERONDALE OMG. I WAS FREAKING OUT! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Honeslty, that was my biggest shock in the book.<br><br>- TESSA. JEM. CLARY. JACE. MAGNUS. ALEC. <br><br>- I really like how the story is building, and I'm eager to read the next book! I love the Shadowhunter universe, and I really like that Cassie keeps adding things we didn't know! The Scholomance really draws my attention, and also the whole world of Faerie! I have a feeling the next books will be even better than this one! Also, I think this is the best first installment of a series Cassie has ever written.<br><br><br>. . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . .<br><br>¿CÓMO QUE HASTA EL 2016? AGHHHHHHH.<br><br>¡Era para el 2015! NOOOOO, CASSIE, NO ME HAGAS ESTO. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420827983ra/13274180.gif" width="400" height="217" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1123355163" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1123355163" />
    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1123355163?book_show_action=true">Dec 04, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=fae">fae</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1123355163" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17951832916959144752"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Entreat me not to leave thee,<br/>Or return from following after thee-<br/>For whither thou goest, I will go”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>The parabatai oath always makes me weep.<br/>By the Angel, my hands are shaking as I'm trying to compose a decent review. I feel broken beyond repair, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/150038.Cassandra_Clare' title='Cassandra Clare' rel='nofollow noopener'>Cassandra Clare</a>'s words ravaged my sanity, shattered my soul and now I'm on my knees searching for tiny fragments, trying to put together what's left of me.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441295812ra/16089989.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I was a child and she was a child,<br/>In this kingdom by the sea,<br/>But we loved wit</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText17951832916959144752" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Entreat me not to leave thee,<br>Or return from following after thee-<br>For whither thou goest, I will go”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The parabatai oath always makes me weep.<br>By the Angel, my hands are shaking as I'm trying to compose a decent review. I feel broken beyond repair, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/150038.Cassandra_Clare" title="Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Cassandra Clare</a>'s words ravaged my sanity, shattered my soul and now I'm on my knees searching for tiny fragments, trying to put together what's left of me.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441295812ra/16089989.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I was a child and she was a child,<br>In this kingdom by the sea,<br>But we loved with a love that was more than love”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>
  <i>Parabatai.</i>
</b> Two warriors bound for life, one soul in two bodies. Your shelter, your friend, your better half. Emma and Julian have always looked out for each other, fought together, chased away the bad dreams, bandaged the physical and the mental wounds. But what happens when this unconditional love turns into something else? Severe punishment, a life apart, a life devoid of meaning. While Emma and the Blackthorns investigate a murderous cult associated with necromantic powers, the stakes are high. Emma can finally find out what happened to her parents and Julian can get his brother back. But when forbidden feelings come to surface, they may endanger everything they hold dear. Their family, their honor, their bond.<br><blockquote>
  <b><i>“We are bound together, Emma, bound together- I breathe when you breathe, I bleed when you bleed, I'm yours and you're mine, you've always been mine, and I have always, </i>always<i> belonged to you!”</i></b>
</blockquote><br>After the Mortal Instruments and the Infernal Devices I thought I was ready for anything <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/150038.Cassandra_Clare" title="Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Cassandra Clare</a> would put me through. After all, I survived <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18335634.Clockwork_Princess__The_Infernal_Devices___3_" title="Clockwork Princess (The Infernal Devices, #3) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Princess</a>' epilogue. Barely. And then came <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25494343.Lady_Midnight__The_Dark_Artifices___1_" title="Lady Midnight (The Dark Artifices, #1) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Lady Midnight</a> and I realized that no power, earthy or heavenly, could have prepared me for this, no iratze could heal my broken heart, no amount of words could possibly describe <b>how much I love this woman, even though she is such a sadist</b>. A terrible, cruel sadist. She can inflict every feeling that crosses your mind, from sorrow and anger and bitterness to elation, hope, happiness and love. Tears of joy, tears of laughter, tears of pain, tears of longing, tears of relief, my eyes were constantly wet.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/534200.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She delivered a story full of <b>action, ass-kicking, suspense and mystery entwined with romance, heartache and the struggles of a broken family to stay together against all odds</b>. An <b>all-entrancing plotline</b> with jaw-dropping moments and hold-your-breath moments and by-the-Angel-I-actually-feel-pity-for-the-villain moments. Ruthless fairies, secrets, bloody lotteries, lies, dark magic and gross demons in a kingdom by the sea, <b>a lost love and a promise for revenge</b>, all of them combined resulted into a mesmerizing tale you never wanted to end. And there's more.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Why all these paintings of you? Because I am an artist, Emma. These pictures are my heart. And if my heart was a canvas, every square inch of it would be painted over with you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>My poor, <i>poor</i> Julian.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459369672ra/18603557.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>A hero worthy of his Herondale blood.</b> Julian was deprived of his childhood, he became a father and a mother to his youngest siblings, he was forced to grow up, be responsible, put aside his wants and needs and bear the weight of the world in his shoulders. He was the glue that kept his family together. He was a gentle soul but ruthless and cunning at the same time, he had to make terrible choices and hide everything he felt. His only refugee was Emma. Stubborn, disobedient, arrogant and wild Emma, who at times was blinded by her need for revenge but cared about Julian so much that made you warm inside. <b>The tension, the longing, the understanding between them gave us a love story that can inspire poems because of its beauty and its tragedy. </b>But every character in this book had a different kind of tragedy to deal with. I was angry at Mark and his ignorance and wrong choices for a long time, but the way he rose to the circumstances won me over. The rest of the Blackthorns were without exceptions amazing characters, and I fought the urge to reach and hug Ty and tell him everything was going to be alright. They deserve alright.<br><br>Of course there was also humour and sassiness that made me burst into loud laughter, and dear Lord the <b>Clace and Malec and Sizzy feels</b> made me squeal! Let me tell you this, Jace became a <i>seriously fine</i> adult. I am and always will be a die-hard Wessa fan but I liked the glimpses at Jem and Tessa, even though my heart was crying for Will. I just miss him so much.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Parabatai.<br>The one who understands your music.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>As for the ending, I have to say only one thing: Emma Cordelia Carstairs, if you proceed with your appalling plan, no power from Heaven or Hell will be able to save you from my wrath.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17951832916959144752" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">
          

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review1123355163">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1942056479?book_show_action=true">Mar 24, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emma Giordano" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emma Giordano" href="/user/show/30604861-emma-giordano">Emma Giordano</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9781442357112" href="/book/show/25813915-lady-midnight">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1942056479" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3523486666221383514">SUCH A GREAT NOVEL THE SECOND TIME AROUND. I'm so happy I decided to reread Lady Midnight. I feel it really helped me get a better grasp on the plot and the characters. I feel so much more in love with this story (as if I was not the first time). I definitely cried so much AGAIN because of all the feels, and I think I have a new found appreciation for certain parts of the story! For example, the inclusion of neurodiverse people in such a conservative society really resonated with me. I was so ha</span>
  <span id="freeText3523486666221383514" style="display:none">SUCH A GREAT NOVEL THE SECOND TIME AROUND. I'm so happy I decided to reread Lady Midnight. I feel it really helped me get a better grasp on the plot and the characters. I feel so much more in love with this story (as if I was not the first time). I definitely cried so much AGAIN because of all the feels, and I think I have a new found appreciation for certain parts of the story! For example, the inclusion of neurodiverse people in such a conservative society really resonated with me. I was so happy to see these individuals standing tall against the stigma enforced by their superiors. I also believe my "ships" are more set in stone this time, as I was not totally committed to a lot of potential romances before. The story was just as powerful, the characters just as loveable, and I'm just gushing at this point because I love Lady Midnight so much. I'm so happy to see Cassie Clare growing so successfully, in her writing and creativity most of all. Now to wallow in sadness for the next SIXTY days while preparing for Lord of Shadows!<br /><br /><i>I received a copy of this book from Simon &amp; Schuster in exchange for an honest review. All opinions are my own.</i></span>

<div id="review_764449819" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/764449819" />
    <a title="C.G. Drews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews"><img alt="C.G. Drews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1521552918p2/11375137.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/764449819?book_show_action=true">Nov 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C.G. Drews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C.G. Drews" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews">C.G. Drews</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=read-2017">read-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=read-2016">read-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=read-2018">read-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=reread">reread</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer764449819" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1705404983111697546"><b>READ #3 | Dec 2018</b><br/><br/>[cue long existential scream of how much I love this book] All I'm saying is that if I had to choose, at knife point, 5 favourite books...this would make the list. <b>I DON'T EVEN KNOW HOW TO SUM UP MY FEELINGS ALRIGHT.</b> 3rd time reading and I am still not ok. I am so wholly and absolutely in love with the Blackthorns and my imagination never never stops with the page, or chapter, or even the novel's end. I just can't let it go. Can't stop thinking about it. This is what I want a b</span>
  <span id="freeText1705404983111697546" style="display:none"><b>READ #3 | Dec 2018</b><br /><br />[cue long existential scream of how much I love this book] All I'm saying is that if I had to choose, at knife point, 5 favourite books...this would make the list. <b>I DON'T EVEN KNOW HOW TO SUM UP MY FEELINGS ALRIGHT.</b> 3rd time reading and I am still not ok. I am so wholly and absolutely in love with the Blackthorns and my imagination never never stops with the page, or chapter, or even the novel's end. I just can't let it go. Can't stop thinking about it. This is what I want a book to make me feel?! Absolutely. everything.<br /><br />(GOD I HAVE SO MANY FEELINGS ABOUT MARK.)<br /><br />(I NEED QOAAD BUT MY PREORDER HAS NOT ARRIVED.)<br /><br /><br />*:·ﾟ✧*:·ﾟ✧<br /><br /><b>READ #2 | MAY 2017</b><br />Omgggg this book has stolen my entire <i>heart</i>. I can't even. I love it <i>more</i> the second time and it's official: THIS IS MY VERY FAVOURITE SHADOWHUNTER BOOK OF THEM ALL. Which is saying something because I love all the Clare books!! My first review still stands true, <b>but here's a smol list of things that really hit me in the reread:</b><br /><br />• Mark Blackthorn is my absolute favourite feral fairy child of them all and I will cut down his enemies and feed him all the warm pretzels.<br />• MARK.<br />• MARRRRRRK<br />• I cannot even with how precious the Blackthorn boys are omg. Julian, who is an anxious father to his 4 little siblings. Mark, who's half in love with a fairy boy and half aching for his family. Ty, who is the most precious and relatable character of my life. Tavvy, who is TOO CUTE THO.<br />• Emma is badass and sassy and I LOVE HER.<br />• Christina is so precious tho.<br />• It's so so funny<br />• Listening to the audio was actually a problem because I SMILED LIKE A DERANGED BAT SO OFTEN I'm sure my family was wondering what even.<br />• most accurate and well-portrayed Autistic character of them all and my heart beats so much for this.<br />• BEST PLOT<br />• I LOVE ALL THE CHARACTERS.<br />• I'M SMITTEN.<br />• SOMEONE REMOVE ME FROM THIS SOBBING PUDDLE I AM IN AND GET ME LORD OF SHADOWS.<br /><br /><br />***<br /><br /><u>
  <b>1ST READ: APRIL 2016</b>
</u><br /><br />The first thing you should know is that <b>I am a permanent rabid Shadowhunter fangirl.</b> EMPHASIS ON THE "RABID" BECAUSE BASICALLY THIS WORLD IS MY LOVE AND I SHALL ADORE EVERYTHING IN IT. Ergo I was doomed to love Lady Midnight. It sooooooo didn't disappoint.<br /><br />So basically I'm about to fangirl ridiculously. #NOTEVENSORRY But at least I'll do it in <i>list format</i> so it can be deranged but sensibly organised. <br /><br /><b>L O V E S: </b><br /><br />• <b>How incredibly awesome EVERYTHING IS.</b><br />*shrieks derrangedly* Okay okay I know that explains nothing, but duuuuude. What isn't perfect about this story?!?! It has <i>everything</i> a Shadowhunter book should have, but this time we're solving a very old murder mystery (the murder of Emma's parents). Plus there's cult stuff going down. Plus there's tons of subplots about "forbidden love". Plus Cassandra Clare's <b>writing just keeps getting better</b> and BETTER. (I loved her first book, but omgggg, I adore it even more now.) Plus everything was fresh and different and interesting despite being the...what?? About 12th Shadowhunter book?? THAT IS AMAZING THAT IS FREAKING AMAZING.<br /><br /><b>• Also I loved Emma and Julian a LOT.</b><br />They're parabanti but, hahhahahahhahaha...<i>they love each other they so totally do</i>. So cue angst and heartbreak. INCOMMMMMING. Emma narrates more than Julian, but I <i>did</i> prefer Julian just because he's really not a black-and-white character. Like he's so GOOD but he's also kind of devious. &lt;3 But subtly so. Whereas Emma is very "let's SMITE THE THING" which is awesome and she was not shallow or boring at all; but she was more open. I did love how Emma was sassy but vulnerable. BUT SASSYYYYYY.<br /><br /><b>• And can we take a moment to love the BIG FAMILY aspect?!?</b><br />How many books do this? Like....not many at all ever. AND HERE WE HAVE AN EPIC FANTASY WITH A HUGE FOCUS ON BIG FAMILY LIFE. *shrieks again* I have a big family so I was like 99% disposed to adore this. So there are 5 Blackthorn children + 2 half fey children. Julian is only 17 but he has basically raised his 4 younger siblings since he was 12. ALONE. TOTALLY ALONE. (Julian precious darling child.) <b>Also I never got the siblings mixed up.</b> They have such distinct personalities. AND they weren't just dumped out of the story. tHEY WERE INVOLVED. They were ADORABLE. THEY ARE MY HEART.<br /><br /><b>• Which leads me to the <i>amazing</i> representation of Autism.</b><br />One of Julian's younger siblings (Ty) has Autism and it's like the most accurate representation I've seen in a LONG time. Omg. I'm so so happy. It's not stereotyped or cliche, there is <i>more</i> to Ty than his Autism, and he is loved and helped despite it. No one talks about curing him. No one talks about how his life would be better without the autism. Ty is awesome and capable and intelligent. IT LIKE ACTUALLY LITERALLY MAKES ME CRY HAPPY TEARS. THANK YOU CASSANDRA CLARE FOR WRITING THIS.<br /><br /><b> • Omggg. There is so much to love. SO MUCH.</b><br />I just...I'm having trouble being SANNNEEEEE. Ahem.<br /><br /><b>• I also loved the secondary characters, <i>of course</i>. </b><br />Cristina is from Mexico and she's pretty dang awesome. Mark is the estranged Blackthorn brother who's been kidnapped/tortured by fey for the last 5 years and he is completely tragic AND I LOVED HIM AND IS QUIET PSYCHOTIC SIDE. Also Malcolm, the resident warlock, continues to be entertaining. And Uncle Arthur was insane. And Church was there. The cat, I mean. Yay church.<br /><br /><b> • Also there ARE plenty of cameos from the other series!</b> <br />Clary and Jace are mentioned several times and make an appearance at the end. Same with Jem and Tessa. And Magnus and Alec...(who are now <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ parrrrents ermagerd!! I SMILED SO MUCH AT THAT PART. They adopted two little boys! Idek why they're not married though??? I was confused that Julian was wondering why they didn't get married. I mean. C'mon. Please humour the shippers. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>) and there's a TEENY TINY short story at the end about Isabelle and Simon's engagement party. <b>So basically it ties everything in and is really sweet.</b><br /><br /><b>• But you COULD read Lady Midnight without having read the rest.</b><br />Just sayin'. It would be better if you at least read The Mortal Instruments though.<br /><br /><b>• I LAUGHED. I CRIED. I AM IN LOVE.</b><br />I need the next book asap.<br /><br /><br /><b> D I S L I K E S:</b><br /><i>(I thought I wouldn't have any, despite it being 5-stars!??!? But I kinda do...)</i><br /><br />•<b> It is way to freaking long.</b><br />I'm kind of terrified because if this is book ONE and it's as big as the TMI finale...omg. #halp It didn't need to be this long, okay? It just didn't. And it hurt my hands to <i>hold</i>. And it did feel tedious at times because it was sooooo loooong. <br /><br /><b> • There was a whole villain monologue at the end which was so cliche!</b><br />I was just surprised! I mean, Emma was keeping The Villain talking so help could arrive but stiiiiill. Not a fan.<br /><br /><b>• I actually thought the stakes would be higher?</b><br />But it could just be because the last book I read EVERYBODY DIED so it was a little disorientating to have less chance of mortal destruction for all here. I mean, BLOOD WAS STILL SHED. YAY. (ahem.) But I was never worried for anyone particularly?<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>BASICALLY!? I LOVED IT AND IT IS FREAKING BRILLIANT.</u>
</b><br />It stole my heart and just made me laugh OUT LOUD several times and afjdlksad I AM RABID SHADOWHUNTER TRASH, THAT IS ALL. I adore the new characters and the big family and the "mystery solving" angle and the deviousness and the plot twists (OMG THE PLOT TWISTS!!!!) and I cannot wait for mooooooore. <br /><br /><br />*** QUOTES ****<br /><br /><blockquote>He'd never seen a teenage girl this excited about anything -- not famous actors, not boy bands, not jewelry. This girl was practically vibrating to pieces over the idea of a dead body. (pg. 11)</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>"We are well known for our jests, japes, and ballads," the faerie said, clearly offended. "Some of our ballads last for weeks."<br />"I don't have that kind of time," Emma said. "I'm a Shadowhunter. Quip fast, die young."</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>As he tucked a fifty into his jeans, Emma noticed that he was wearing a gray T-shirt that said TMI on the front. "Too much information?" she said. <br />He brightened. "The Mortal Instruments. They're a band. From Brooklyn. You heard of them?"</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>Ty said nothing. His hands were still fluttering in their repetitive movements. There had been a time when Ty's father had tried to train him to immobility, had held his sons' hands tightly at his sides when he was upset and said, "Still, <i>still</i>". It had panicked Ty into throwing up. Julian never did that. He just said everyone got butterflies when they were nervous; some people got them in their stomaches, and Ty showed them in his hands. (pg. 142)</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>"Mark. Mark!" She waved the wallet over her head. "This is a clue. An actual <i>clue</i>. I think I love you."<br />Mark's eyebrows went up. "In faerie, if you said that, we would have to pledge our troth, and you might put a <i>geas</i> upon me that I would not stray from you or I would die."<br />Emma shoved the wallet in her pocket. "Well, here it's just an expression that means 'I like you very much' or even 'Thanks for the bloodstained wallet.'" (pg. 212) </blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>"This is <i>my</i> domain." You've got your own hopeless humans in New York."<br />"One of those hopeless humans is the father of my child," Magnus pointed out.</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote> <i>It's not his fault if he doesn't understand everything. Or if things are too much for him. It's not his fault.</i> </blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>Julian had looked at his own inexact, messy work and Ty's methodical rows, and thought: <i>We both see the same world, but in a different way. Ty feels the same joy I do, the joy of creation. We feel all the same things, only the shape of our feelings are different.</i> </blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote> Emma giggled. "You told him Shadowhunters are DIY about their killing?"<br />"We're DIY about <i>everything.</i>" (pg. 251)</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote> "Why did you pull the arrow out?" she demanded...<br />Jule's breath was coming in harsh pants. "Because when someone -- shoots you with an arrow --" he gasps, "your immediate response is not -- 'thanks for the arrow, I think I'll keep it for a while'."<br />"Good to know your sense of humour is still intact."</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>"You're too skinny," she said as brightly as she could. "Too much coffee, not enough pancakes."<br />"I hope they put that on my tombstone."</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>"And why is Tavvy in a bag of sugar?"<br />Mark shrugged. "He wanted to be in a bag of sugar."<br />"That doesn't mean you should <i>put</i> him in a bag of sugar." Julian's voice rose.</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>"Why are all these paintings of you? Because I'm an artist, Emma. These pictures are my heart. And if my heart was a canvas, every square inch of it would be painted over with you."</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>"Well, either you've been out fighting the forces of evil or you've come from a much wilder party than we have," Jace said.</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="1705404983111697546" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
