<div id="review_2435531671" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2435531671" />
    <a title="Elle (ellexamines)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/52545435-elle-ellexamines"><img alt="Elle (ellexamines)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1582250895p2/52545435.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2435531671?book_show_action=true">Jun 25, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elle (ellexamines)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elle (ellexamines)" href="/user/show/52545435-elle-ellexamines">Elle (ellexamines)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781481475266" href="/book/show/27788505-lady-midnight">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52545435-elle-ellexamines?shelf=favorite-relationships">favorite-relationships</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52545435-elle-ellexamines?shelf=favorite-friendships">favorite-friendships</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52545435-elle-ellexamines?shelf=gay-genre-fiction">gay-genre-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52545435-elle-ellexamines?shelf=villain-antihero-arcs">villain-antihero-arcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52545435-elle-ellexamines?shelf=sff-pn-urban-fantasy">sff-pn-urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52545435-elle-ellexamines?shelf=z-read2018">z-read2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52545435-elle-ellexamines?shelf=y-out2016">y-out2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52545435-elle-ellexamines?shelf=favorite-characters">favorite-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52545435-elle-ellexamines?shelf=z-faves2018">z-faves2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52545435-elle-ellexamines?shelf=favorite-squads">favorite-squads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2435531671" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5861981505369926461">like, I'm glad I enjoyed this, but wow fuck you guys this broke my heart and the only thing I got out of it was my <a href='https://incorrecttdaquotes.tumblr.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>new favorite tumblr blog</a><br/><br/>So, uh, it turns out I like Cassandra Clare books now, and I think she's just improved significantly at creating lovable characters and narratives I personally find compelling, and I am so glad I have learned to love this.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>dark artifices reviews:</i>
</b> <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2435531671' rel='nofollow noopener'>book one</a> | <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2569455643' rel='nofollow noopener'>book two</a> | <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2575341745' rel='nofollow noopener'>book three</a><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>➽P L O T A N D T H E M E S</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><b>The villain of this book is hate and oppr</b></span>
  <span id="freeText5861981505369926461" style="display:none">like, I'm glad I enjoyed this, but wow fuck you guys this broke my heart and the only thing I got out of it was my <a href="https://incorrecttdaquotes.tumblr.com" rel="nofollow noopener">new favorite tumblr blog</a><br><br>So, uh, it turns out I like Cassandra Clare books now, and I think she's just improved significantly at creating lovable characters and narratives I personally find compelling, and I am so glad I have learned to love this.<br><br><b>
  <i>dark artifices reviews:</i>
</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2435531671" rel="nofollow noopener">book one</a> | <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2569455643" rel="nofollow noopener">book two</a> | <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2575341745" rel="nofollow noopener">book three</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>➽P L O T A N D T H E M E S</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>The villain of this book is hate and oppression.</b> The amount of clave-dragging in here…… I’ve been waiting for literal years. And though I think this becomes much more clear in book two, it’s clear from the beginning that hate is about to be the villain. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“This is why fairies are despised, this senseless cruelty.”<br>“Careful, boy,” said Gwynn. “You have your laws and we have ours. The difference is that we do not pretend ours are not cruel.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><i>Lady Midnight</i> follows various characters and plotlines, most notably including our Forbidden Romantic Plotline, our The Cold Peace Is Terrible plotline, and our Julian Gets Repeatedly Fucked Over By The Clave plotline, but every plotline has a common villain: systematic prejudice. <br><br>Also, can I just say: I can’t believe the main villain of this series is a Donald Trump allegory. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>➽E M M A A N D J U L I A N</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>✔Emma Carstairs - a literal ICON, invented big dick energy<br>✔Julian Blackthorn - definitely would kill a man for his own selfish motivations but listen… he's in love with Emma, that's too relatable and therefore i can't hate him<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1540754541i/26513203._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="http://inejgayfa.tumblr.com/post/179003253881/cassandraclare-emmilinne-this-was-just-a" rel="nofollow noopener">[source for both]</a><br><br>I literally love that the main couple of this is a reversed bad boy / good girl who’s maybe turning evil dynamic. It’s this strange dynamic because this author <i>feeds into this trope</i>, and seeing such a conscious subversion of that ideal in her work was incredible. There’s this one line where the female lead is like “oh this is his first kiss meanwhile I’ve slept with like 20 people but that’s okay it’s us” and I was SCREAMING I can’t believe this book killed slutshaming. Anyway, I love this so much I’m obsessed with it. <br><br>Also, their relationship is <i>so tense</i>. Like, the mutual pining is too good. Also, please let me just share this meme I’ve been laughing at for three years:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1538971227i/26415503._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I will actually admit that I did not like Emma and Julian’s dynamic… quite as much in the next book, which I talked about <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2569455643" rel="nofollow noopener">in my review</a>? BUT OH WELL.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>➽K I E R A N, M A R K, C H R I S T I N A </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>✔Christina Rosales - an ICON, a blessing to my life………. I love that she’s close platonic friends with Emma and they never feud, I love how much she asks for herself and how unapologetic she is about her life, I just relate to her a lot and I hope she’s happy forever<br>✔Mark Blackthorn - my boy, my man, the bi icon we deserved. I actually loved his entire reintegration arc so so so much and I <i>adore</i> that he’s trapped between two worlds but still doing his best to get back within his home. too good we did not deserve him<br>✔Kieran of the Hunt - did anyone try the chicken? I thought the chicken was lovely. book two Kieran is the superior Kieran and that’s my discourse for the day. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1540754541i/26513202._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="http://inejgayfa.tumblr.com/post/179003253881/cassandraclare-emmilinne-this-was-just-a" rel="nofollow noopener">[source for both]</a><br><br>I’m sorry, but if we’re going to talk about Cassandra Clare redoing constructs from her own work in a different way: the three-sided love triangle of Kieran and Christina and Mark. I will <i>not</i> be elaborating on which dynamic this echoes at this time. <br><br>In other news, I cried <i>twice</i> during this book, and both times it was about - you guessed it - Mark and Kieran’s backstory!! They didn’t have to do me like this. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Kieran didn’t have to do anyone like this. INCLUDING ME that line where he was like “I cannot bear it” Kieran can’t lie he’s not lying he literally means that. in other news I fucking hate this <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>➽T H E B L A C K T H O R N S</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>✔Diana Wrayburn - genuinely one of my favorite characters from this series and i have NO IDEA why she’s so slept on. i mean, it’s not like anyone hates her, but i would like you all to be screaming about Diana for 40 hours per week as i do? this is a full-time Diana love zone. i love my canonically trans wife<br>✔Taavy Blackthorn - he’s ten and i’m pretty sure ten year olds don’t have personalities. pure. <br>✔Dru Blackthorn - I would fucking die for Dru she’s too legendary. also, she’s plus-sized and the narrative is so good about it. <br>✔Livvy Blackthorn - a small bean doing her best and it’s just not very good.<br>✔Ty Blackthorn - deliciousfinallysomegoodfuckingfood.gif it is really, really depressing how few books have canonically autistic characters who are not essentially used as jokes, but here we are. <br>✔Kit <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Herondale <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> - chaotic bisexual. i have a tumblr post to share about this involving the phrase “token straight family member” but unfortunately, spoilers. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[what is up with this whole plot twist about someone being a Herondale motif. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>In case you haven’t noticed, <b>I love the Blackthorn family.</b> The dynamic of the siblings with Julian is absolutely the best, and their mutual love and support for each other means so much to me. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You pointed a knife at me.” <br>“It wasn’t personal.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Soooooo, Ty and Kit had two separate meet cutes in this and both of them were the best thing I’ve ever read. They definitely get more development in book two, but Kit’s joining-the-Blackthorns arc, even here, was absolutely the best. Basically, <a href="http://inejgayfa.tumblr.com/post/179283710279/tiberiusblacktorn-social-media-edit-livvy-kit" rel="nofollow noopener">I really wish I could continue to be emotional about the Blackthorns forever.</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>➽O T H E R C H A R A C T E R S</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>✔Diego Rosales - not nearly as perfect as the marketing would indicate but I actually him?<br>✔Annabelle Blackthorn - a very very interesting character of book two. <br>✔Zara Dearborn - a very very awful character of book two. fuck off, Zara. <br><br>I think we all know Cassandra Clare is really into the overlaps between worlds, and I’m honestly… here for it. Jace and Clary’s cameo is the most I’ve liked them in the entire canon of the universe. Jem and Tessa showed up for three pages and it was my favorite thing I’ve ever read. There was some line about the Carstairs “owing the Herondales” and I feel like that’s the exact opposite of TID canon but okay? <br><br><s>also, I know I’m a bitch, but Tessa and Jem were not in book two, and I think that makes it a bad book, personally</s><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>➽S H U T U P, E L L E</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>ANYWAY, the point is, I really enjoyed this book, and so far I'm really enjoying this series. I hope I will continue to not die of sadness!!<br><br><b>
  <i>dark artifices reviews:</i>
</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2435531671" rel="nofollow noopener">book one</a> | <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2569455643" rel="nofollow noopener">book two</a> | <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2575341745" rel="nofollow noopener">book three</a><br><br><a href="https://thebookishactress.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/52545435" rel="nofollow noopener">Goodreads</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/jespergayhey" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/thebookishactress/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="http://www.youtube.com/channel/UCVIY_GxZIuclzsIw9CLSe3g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1283993828" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1283993828" />
    <a title="alexandra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6784858-alexandra"><img alt="alexandra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1592456461p2/6784858.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1283993828?book_show_action=true">May 18, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="alexandra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="alexandra" href="/user/show/6784858-alexandra">alexandra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6784858-alexandra?shelf=ss">ss</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6784858-alexandra?shelf=feelz">feelz</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6784858-alexandra?shelf=own-in-physical-form">own-in-physical-form</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6784858-alexandra?shelf=faves">faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6784858-alexandra?shelf=signed">signed</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6784858-alexandra?shelf=arc-physical">arc-physical</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1283993828" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4121074701002272880"><b>FULL REVIEW + DISCUSSION ON <a href='http://www.twirlingpages.com/2016/03/08/review-discussion-lady-midnight-cassandra-clare/' rel='nofollow noopener'>twirlingpages.com!</a></b><br/><br/>2/2/2016 : well, i feel like my soul shattered into a billion pieces and blew into the ocean. how will i ever recover from this novel???? or this ending?????? <em>i won't.</em> good bye world. i drowned in my own tears and my entire being fell into shambles thanks to this FANTASTIC novel. i need the next one NOW, even though this one hasn't even released yet... oops.<br/><br/>*clears throat* okay, saying LADY MIDNGHT is an emotional rollercoaster ride is an understatem</span>
  <span id="freeText4121074701002272880" style="display:none"><b>FULL REVIEW + DISCUSSION ON <a href="http://www.twirlingpages.com/2016/03/08/review-discussion-lady-midnight-cassandra-clare/" rel="nofollow noopener">twirlingpages.com!</a></b><br /><br />2/2/2016 : well, i feel like my soul shattered into a billion pieces and blew into the ocean. how will i ever recover from this novel???? or this ending?????? <em>i won't.</em> good bye world. i drowned in my own tears and my entire being fell into shambles thanks to this FANTASTIC novel. i need the next one NOW, even though this one hasn't even released yet... oops.<br /><br />*clears throat* okay, saying LADY MIDNGHT is an emotional rollercoaster ride is an understatement. i'm shell-shocked by cassandra clare's improvement in writing, world building, character development, EVERYTHING. especially since i just finished rereading her first two novels, it's so obviously clear as to how much she's grown as an author. she keeps getting better and better.<br /><br />my favorite part of LADY MIDNIGHT is not the intricately thought out plot – which is very intricate and very fantastic – but the depth of our cast. i remember reading THE MORTAL INSTRUMENTS and finding everyone a bit flat or "too perfect." clary and jace (from TMI) were both born to be legends and, to me, they were cutouts of The Chosen One. our main characters in LM, emma and julian, aren't naturally "special" but work to where they're at. i could easily connect with them because they're just regular people, erm, shadowhunters, who are trying to make the most out of what's come out of the war. and it's not only our two leads who i adore; EVERYONE is incredibly fleshed out and unique. clare made it so easy for me to connect with all of them, which led me to feel ALL THE FEELZ. i also love how there are many diverse characters and aspects, but they weren't the main focus; it's there and it's important but it's not flung in your face.<br /><br />cassandra clare's ability to create more depth in the shadow world never fazes to amaze me. i personally don't find the writing to be very special, but THE WORLD is so incredible. we see characters we know from TMI and TID (which made me SO GIDDY), but also see the back story to minor characters in the other series. more secrets about their government unravel, more family relationships explained, and MORE ANGST. it's also nice because it's written in a way that doesn't require you to read the companion series. <br /><br />the plot has such a nice balance between action, romance, suspense, and magic. although the book is the size of a monster, there weren't many parts that felt dragged or unnecessary (a few, but not many). one of the conflicts of the story follows family relationships and the like, which i LOVE because i feel like there's more to YA drama than romance and monsters; LADY MIDNIGHT has all three! *sly grin* but yes, this book has a perfect mix of everything.<br /><br />if you couldn't tell from my paragraphs of gushing, I LOVE THIS NOVEL. i usually try to be very picky and critical with my books, but i honestly couldn't find anything i truly disliked. it made me fall in love with the world and characters and everything about everything. (it also made me feel like i was being stabbed in the heart a few million times, but i suppose i'm a bit masochistic.) and now, i'm going to reread all of cassie clare's other novels and allow this world to consume my soul &lt;3333</span>
  <a data-text-id="4121074701002272880" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_450057358" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/450057358" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8429172-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595453256p2/8429172.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/450057358?book_show_action=true">Nov 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/8429172-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=ugh">ugh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=girl-crush">girl-crush</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=ebooks-i-own">ebooks-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8429172-laura?shelf=damn-pretty-covers">damn-pretty-covers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer450057358" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14336547864185081330"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420429845ra/13223235.gif' width='500' height='245' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>"Lex malla, lex nulla. <i>A bad law is no law."</i></b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>This could be one of the hardest reviews I’ve ever written and that’s just because my feelings and thoughts are all over the place and I know, no matter how many days pass, I won’t be able to have a clear response so bear with me. <b>This is going to be a mess.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448129384ra/17098893.gif' width='500' height='207' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>As usual, there were things I liked and things I didn’t. In this particular case, I don’t know if everything I loved can outweigh what I disliked. This is the first time I had to call two of my </span>
  <span id="freeText14336547864185081330" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420429845ra/13223235.gif" width="500" height="245" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"Lex malla, lex nulla. <i>A bad law is no law."</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>This could be one of the hardest reviews I’ve ever written and that’s just because my feelings and thoughts are all over the place and I know, no matter how many days pass, I won’t be able to have a clear response so bear with me. <b>This is going to be a mess.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448129384ra/17098893.gif" width="500" height="207" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As usual, there were things I liked and things I didn’t. In this particular case, I don’t know if everything I loved can outweigh what I disliked. This is the first time I had to call two of my friends to ask them if I was being neutral enough and this is the result.<br><br>If at this point y’all don’t know this is not a spoiler free blog and therefore my reviews contain untagged spoilers, then I don’t know what you guys are up to. Read at your own risk.<br><br>Lady Midnight is the first book in what is going to be a trilogy named The Dark Artifices and in this first installment, we deal with the aftermath of the Dark War that, after 5 years, it still has a huge impact in the Shadowhunter world. We follow Emma Carstairs and Julian Blackthorn as they work together to discover who’s behind the murders of mundanes and faeries happening in Los Angeles.<br><br>Now, I’m going to begin with what I actually liked about this book because I feel like I need to start with positive things.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458433423ra/18488554.gif" width="500" height="274" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>•I absolutely adored the Blackthorn dynamic. I really like this family a lot! I loved how close they are and how they manage all the situations they get themselves involved. I think they could’ve been written really poorly but I’m so happy with all of them. I love Julian and his strong sense of responsibility, I love Ty and his way of seeing things<i>(I don’t know exactly his condition; it can be a grade of autism, though I don’t know if people can have just a bit of it or it can also be Asperger syndrome but I was glad to read about a character like that and that person being an actual active member of everything)</i> and Livvy with her fierceness, Dru with her love for morbid topics and how protective she was of Tavvy and Tavvy being so young and cute and I just really loved them all. And Mark, who I actually got to know a bit in Bitter of Tongue, I grew to like him a lot in this book.<br><br>•Dude, I fucking loved Cristina Mendoza Rosales. She was such a mature character and she gave me and a lot of people new perspectives and while she was a rule follower, she was ready for everything and understood there were things higher than law and I just fell for her so hard. I’m just happy she exists.<br><br>•I loved reading about all characters and their cameos and it was a big fangirl moment for me. Jace actually seemed to have grown up a lot and reading about Izzy and Simon’s engagement party and Tessa and Jem, holy shit, I was so <b>so happy</b> and *sighs*so good.<br><br>•Cristina and Mark are my new ship and I will sink with them. I’m so here for more of those two. You have no idea how much I ship them omg.<br>And that was about it. If I end up reading the second book, when it comes out, it’ll be only for what I wrote above. <br><br>Now comes the part where I rant about everything I actually hated so if <u>you loved the book,</u> you may want to stop reading this now.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458433423ra/18488555.gif" width="245" height="246" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Boy, I was not pleased with A LOT of things and it made so sad. For 4 years since it was announced this trilogy was coming out and after we all met the characters when they were children, I was sold. <br>I’m telling you, after City of Heavenly Fire, I was ready to take a break. Since 2010 I was reading CC’s books nonstop and I was exhausted. You all know these books got centuries worth of baggage and I was going to wait until The Dark Artifices had at least 2 books out, you know? And then these kids came into the picture and I couldn’t help it. I had to know what was going to be for them in the future.<br><br>Enter Lady Midnight and just nah.<br><br>Probably one of things I hated the most was how in-your-face was the whole romance between Emma and Julian because for years we were sold the idea of how unthinkable was a romance between parabatai and I expected so much and more from this book and I didn’t get it at all.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458433423ra/18488556.gif" width="500" height="208" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don’t know if I was misguided or maybe it was just me but I thought that, <i>at least in this first book,</i> Julian’s feelings were going to be unrequired. So color me surprise when it was not Julian who I first read having doubts about it but Emma. <b>In the first fucking chapter.</b> I was like whaaaat??? And from there the romance went downhill for me. It’s not the fact that Emma loved him too, no. It is just that there was not mystery. There was not seduction. CC did not play with the possibilities when we all were expecting being heartbroken and this impossible love for so many reasons and I did not get it. I’m not even talking about Emma and Julian having sex at the first opportunity but rather the notion of them thinking it was not going to affect their parabatai bond. It was how poorly it was handled. It was because the level of ridiculousness shocked the fuck out of me. <br><br>I’d like to think I’m not the only one who feels that their romance was not only was rushed but also bad written and I just got this incredible feeling of being tricked and robbed. And while I wasn’t crazy for all the angst I knew it gotta exist because, hello parabatai in love, I was not expecting them got their feelings somewhat sorted out that quick. Sue me, I like to be seduced but nooo.<br><br>Which leads me to the thing I hated the most…<br><br>Are. You. Freaking. Kidding. Me? I knew, as soon as Julian was hurt and Emma put that iratze on him and shit worked amazingly, something was up. And what was it? <i>Well, apparently when the pair of parabatai fall in love, their runes become even more powerful because….</i> yeah, I guess romantic love is the most powerful thing in the world. Bullshit.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449344781ra/17271436.gif" width="500" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you ask me, two parabatai who are siblings, have more chances of being all powerful because a) they share blood b) they grew up together c) parabatai bond. To me, that’s a killer combination <b>if you’re following the CC’s logic.</b> But nope, romantic love y’all.<br><br>And the reason why parabatai can’t be romantically together? They become all magic powerful and go Hercules on everyone around them. Like, killing everyone and going power crazy.<br><br><u>
  <i>How convenient that was never mentioned.</i>
</u> A friend of mine told me she read something about a Lightwood being in love with their parabatai and the result was mortal to them back before The Infernal Devices and that’s it. And now Lady Midnight. <br><br>I just hate how everything was left out, how there was no information about this until now. How. Fucking. Convenient. <br><br>It’s feels like when someone tells you <i> “oops, you should have read the fine print”</i> because I don’t remember reading anything in the Codex about such thing. And one would think something so important would’ve been included in the Codex no matter how "in the shadows" that shit had to stay. Actually, the parabatai part in the Codex was absurdly short and most of it was the vow. <br><br><b>Something so important and sacred for this world has so little information. How convenient. Next thing we’ll know it’s a way to break the parabatai bond without any of them being dead because the power of true love.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458433423ra/18488557.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I’m frustrated and mad. How dare CC to take such an already established concept, a concept we all already know about and it’s so important and twist it to her better convenience? Just no. How disrespectful of her.<br><br>And some of you may say “but they’re her books and she can do what she wants…” yes but that’s not how shit goes and we all know it. It’s really not fair to change the rules at this point just because it’s easier that way.<br><br>And the way Emma broke things with Julian? Fuck.<br><br>Why does she have to involve Mark? Doesn’t she realize Julian is going to end up hating Mark and therefore the brothers are going to be divided and that’s going to divide the siblings and it’s going to hurt everyone but mostly Julian? Doesn’t she realize how selfish that decision was? Couldn’t she just break things with Julian and try to “date” someone else? Why create unnecessary drama?<br><br>Emma spent the whole book saying and proving she cares a great deal about Julian, duh she loves him, but she just doesn’t think about the consequences. She doesn’t think about Mark having to deal with Julian’s feelings, too. <br><br>She doesn’t think about Mark having small feeling for Cristina. She doesn’t think about her friend liking Mark, too. She doesn’t stop to think about anything and yes, you may tell me “but Laura, she didn’t force him" and you’re right! But as soon as she said it was to help Julian, we all know Mark was game and that isn’t fair.<br><br>Now, let’s leave Emma and Julian aside for a while and let’s talk about the main villain in this book.<br> <br>So, Malcom Fade, High Warlock of Los Angeles. Someone so in love with someone, so hurt by betrayal and so powerful he managed to kill a lot of people and form a cult for years in order to bring back to life his old love. <br><br>I just didn’t feel it. I don’t know if it was because we didn’t know Malcom that much so the fact that he turned out being the bad guy, while surprising, didn’t evoke a lot of things to me. I mean, yeah, he turned out <i>hating</i> the kids he saw grow and poor kids, you know? But that was it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458433423ra/18488558.gif" width="500" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Everything about this plot was weak and I get that Emma’s parents ended up being just meaningless deaths and that’s something she will have to deal with but I just was not impressed by Malcom trying to rise Anabel from the dead. I feel like it was such a hollow thing. Maybe because I’m used to bad guys trying to destroy everything and conquer the world that here came this guy and he only wanted to be with his beloved one again and some of the Fair Folk helping him, it still didn’t work out in my opinion. It was something so bizarre like this kid Christopher Herondale.<br><br>Fuck me sideways, I thought Tessa and Jem were looking for powerful <b>artifice</b> but this kid? While I’m in love with William Herondale and the mere mention of him can bring me to my knees, this plot twist was uncalled for and stupid. Is CC trying to win people over? Someone please give me a valid reason why this kid is needed? And I know we don’t have Herondale representation, I know. Jace may be called Herondale but he was raised Lightwood. So if the only reason why this kid was brought was to be a plot device, then I’m out.<br><br>Guys, I’m confused and mad and disappointed. I just don’t see a way out.<br><br>What can let Emma and Julian be together? Well, one of them could become a supernatural creature. That way the parabatai bond would break and they could be together.<br><br>Or they can be exiled and stripped from their Marks and if they survive that, then yeah, cool.<br><br>Or they could die in the process.<br><br><u>BUT if later in the books a way for them to be together is discovered while still being both Shadowhunters and alive, after everything we’ve been told, then what’s the fucking point?</u><br><br>I’m not happy with this book, as you can see and I just don’t know what to make out of it.<br><br>I'm not happy with how childish it was. One would think CC has grown as a writer <i>(I just laughed so hard omg)</i> so much in the past years that she's now capable of delivering mature content but no. High school drama going on here.<br><br>I know I left a lot of things out in this review but it’d take me forever to tell you about every single thing I hated.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="14336547864185081330" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin" href="/user/show/17438949-melissa-dog-wolf-lover-martin">Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1510315563" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17474967833254007326"><b>Update: $3.99 Kindle US today only 8-20-17</b><br/><br/>Okay so I'm just going to put the ole spoiler beware up here because I think I'm just going to start spoiling on most every book I read so that I can talk to myself about it. Ya get meh? ❤<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454099516i/17918639._SX540_.jpg' alt=' : ' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Okay so I loved, loved, loved that there were parts that had Jem and Tessa from The Infernal Devices in it. I love them and I loved Jem so much so it was really touching. I liked that it had some parts where Clary, Jace, Magnus and Alex were in it. Not so much as Jem an</span>
  <span id="freeText17474967833254007326" style="display:none"><b>Update: $3.99 Kindle US today only 8-20-17</b><br><br>Okay so I'm just going to put the ole spoiler beware up here because I think I'm just going to start spoiling on most every book I read so that I can talk to myself about it. Ya get meh? ❤<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454099516i/17918639._SX540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Okay so I loved, loved, loved that there were parts that had Jem and Tessa from The Infernal Devices in it. I love them and I loved Jem so much so it was really touching. I liked that it had some parts where Clary, Jace, Magnus and Alex were in it. Not so much as Jem and Tessa because they are just better to me. <br><br>I am absolutely in love with Mark, ❤ the half faerie half shadowhunter that was taken in the last book of the mortal instruments. He had to go to the faerie realm because of reasons and now he's back to try to help the Blackthorns and Emma find who are murdering faeries and such. If he completes this trial and they find the murderer then he can have the choice of staying with his family or going back to the Wild Hunt. &lt;--- It's a faerie thing you can read about it. <br><br>Emma Carstairs, who is a distant relation to Jem (swoon), is living with the Blackthorns because Julian Blackthorn is her parabatai. Their uncle is supposed to be running the home/institute but it's really Julian and he also takes care of all his siblings. I loved all of them too. The only thing that got on my nerves was how many times they had to mention they were parabatai. I wanted to scream we know already. But, I digress. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1486482479i/21919185._SY540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1486482479i/21919186._SX540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But then they start falling for each other and that is forbidden. It's a LAW! And it seems for good reason as Jem states to Emma at the end of the book. Thank goodness. I really wanted Emma to end up with Mark because he's hot and he's a little wild like Emma. Then I thought he was going to want Emma's best friend Cristina. Then find out he's with some faerie dude. So, no I wasn't happy with any of this. But, the ending might lead to what I'm hoping for! <br><br>Emma is bad to the bone. She has trained since she was little. She really kicks arse and she's not a brat. I never wanted to smack her like I did Clary in all the other books. Emma is a tough warrior and does everything she can to help every one else. <br><br>Everyone is trying to find out about these murders. The little kids are doing research online while the others go out and look for clues. Julian almost dies when he gets shot with a poisoned arrow but Emma saves him. <br><br>Emma and Mark go out on their own on his steed and find more clues and kill some demons. <br><br>They also have a warlock friend named Malcolm, he helps out where he can. See none of them are supposed to be helping the faeries so it's all hush-hush. It's a law and they could get in trouble with the Clave after the Cold War 5 years ago when they set up some more laws. Sigh. They help anyway because the same markings that are on the dead were on Emma's parents when they were brutally killed. Plus, they want Mark back, if he wants to come back. <br><br>Turns out there some cult out there that put people in a lottery and if they are chosen they have to go kill someone. And there are reasons. They have a Guardian that wants this done for reasons and I didn't even see it coming when I found out who the Guardian was.... I can definitely understand the Guardians reasons for doing what they were doing. I felt sad for Emma when she found out and also glad because she killed the Guardian. Although, they will probably not be dead for real. They will come creeping back in the next book! <br><br>Speaking of the next book! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1486482479ra/21919187.gif" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Something wicked this way comes! I'm going to assume there will be hell on earth because when you take an innocent person and do what they did to them . . . um, yeah . . . I would think the Kraken is going to be released! I can't wait to see =)<br><br>MY BLOG: <a href="http://melissa413readsalot.blogspot.com/2017/02/lady-midnight-by-cassandra-clare.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Melissa Martin's Reading List</a></span>

<div id="review_1438462717" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1438462717" />
    <a title="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44137919-mikee-readwithmikee"><img alt="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583262285p2/44137919.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1438462717?book_show_action=true">Nov 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" href="/user/show/44137919-mikee-readwithmikee">Mikee (ReadWithMikee)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1438462717" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8117516673261087863"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457812086i/18409404._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The stars wheeled crazily overhead as she spun, sucking in her breath as her body slowed its rolling. She came to a stop on her back, her hair and clothes full of sand and her ears full of the sound of the wildly crashing ocean…”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><b>To the people who say that Cassandra Clare is dragging this on, milking the cow, etc:</b> PLEASE STOP. There's people all over the world who are grateful for these books and series. Don't ruin it for everyone else. You don't have to like Cassie. You don't have t</span>
  <span id="freeText8117516673261087863" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457812086i/18409404._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The stars wheeled crazily overhead as she spun, sucking in her breath as her body slowed its rolling. She came to a stop on her back, her hair and clothes full of sand and her ears full of the sound of the wildly crashing ocean…”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><b>To the people who say that Cassandra Clare is dragging this on, milking the cow, etc:</b> PLEASE STOP. There's people all over the world who are grateful for these books and series. Don't ruin it for everyone else. You don't have to like Cassie. You don't have to read her books. But at least have some respect for the author and her loyal readers. Prior to reading The Mortal Instruments and The Infernal Devices, I too criticized the fact that Cassie only wrote books within her Shadowhunter world. Once I got a taste of a world full of Nephilim, runes, parabatai, and seraph blades, I quickly (and proudly) ate those words up without hesitation. We all have books we love, books we hate. No one should be shamed for the books they choose to read. Just as authors shouldn't be shamed for the world that the create. People complain about underdeveloped world-building and now people are complaining about "overdevelopment". Let it be. Don't read the books. Don't spend your money. But don't drag the author, their hard work, their imagination, and the readers who love to support their creation. End of rant.<br><br>Anyways...<br><br>Words can't even describe how much hype surrounded this book. But you know what... Lady Midnight was so much better than I ever would have comprehended. Lady Midnight was not <b>
  <i>just great.</i>
</b> It was not <b>
  <i>just amazing.</i>
</b> It was not <b>
  <i>just fantastic.</i>
</b> There were absolutely <b>
  <u>NO WORDS</u>
</b> to describe the masterpiece that this book was. Every word, every sentence, every punctuation had me hooked to the very core to the point where putting this book down was <b>torture.</b><br><br>The Infernal Devices will probably always be my favorite Shadowhunter series but after putting this book down, I'm left doubting if that statement even proves to be true anymore. I even predicted that The Dark Artfices would put The Mortal Instruments to shame. Boy, I was wrong. Lady Midnight completely <b>
  <i>obliterated</i>
</b> The Mortal Instruments. Clary <i>
  <b>who?</b>
</i> Jace <i>
  <b>who?</b>
</i> Because after being reintroduced to these characters, I forgot all about The Mortal Instruments and the characters that preceded Emma and Julian five years earlier.<br><br>Emma Carstairs was fierce. Determined. Every bit as <b>
  <u>BADASS</u>
</b> as a heroine should be. I was never annoyed with her like I was with Clary because unlike Clary, Emma actually knew <b>
  <u>how to listen.</u>
</b> She knew her limits and when to stop. It was actually refreshing after putting up with bratty Clary for six books.<br><br>As for Julian Blackthorn -- he made this book for me. I absolutely adored him. <b>Julian Blackthorn could do no wrong</b> in my eyes. I felt so much for him and how he had to grow up at such a young age to be the father to Livvy, Tiberius, Dru, and Tavvy. My heart broke for him so many times. He is not quite like Will or Jace Herondale. If anything, Julian Blackthorn has the <b>
  <i>outward appearance of Will and Jace, but the heart and personality of Jem and Alec.</i>
</b><br><br>I very much enjoyed how this book finally decided to explore the law behind why <b>parabatai should never fall in love.</b> It was a detail that I've been wondering from the moment the term parabatai was introduced to us. The romance in Lady Midnight was steamy, complicated, and all the while... <b>
  <i>heartbreaking.</i>
</b> Especially after that ending. I loved the friendship between Emma and Julian ever since they were introduced in City of Heavenly Fire. I had a feeling that their hasty decision of becoming parabatai would prove to be problematic in the future and boy did it get <b>
  <i>messy</i>
</b> in Lady Midnight. The tension between Emma and Julian throughout this whole book was just so thick it drove me <b>
  <u>CRAZY.</u>
</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>However, as much as I ship Emma and Julian I guiltily ship Emma and Mark as well. There I said it! But can you blame me? This book literally has a love pentagon.<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Lady Midnight was just perfect from beginning to end. From its beautiful cover, to the plot, the romance, everything! It all weaves together seamlessly. I can't wait to see how everything unfolds in this new chapter of the Shadowhunter world.<br><br><b>P.S. I love you Cassie but after that ending, I just want to jump off a cliff and drag you along with me. <i>WHY OH WHY DO YOU LOVE TO DO THIS TO US?</i> I'd take a million of your lengthy epilogues over this one page epilogue that left me reeling!</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="8117516673261087863" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/295136436?book_show_action=true">Mar 15, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Haleema" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Haleema" href="/user/show/4336293-haleema">Haleema</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4336293-haleema?shelf=pretentious">pretentious</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4336293-haleema?shelf=cheese">cheese</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4336293-haleema?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4336293-haleema?shelf=not-again">not-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4336293-haleema?shelf=bad-writing">bad-writing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4336293-haleema?shelf=half-wit-characters">half-wit-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4336293-haleema?shelf=predictable">predictable</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer295136436" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14249772582539805012">So I take a almost a two-year hiatus from reading, and I do this. I come back to one of the wretched Shadowhunter series. I was waiting to get my car fixed at Walmart a few days ago, and I decided to pick this book up. I don't know what I was expecting...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403452726ra/10095198.gif' width='180' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>There are at least a few common things you can find in every Shadowhunter series.<br/><br/>1. Forbidden love or love triangle of some sort<br/>2. Lots of angst but the bad kind<br/>3. Long, awkward, and often cringe descriptions of make out sessions between love in</span>
  <span id="freeText14249772582539805012" style="display:none">So I take a almost a two-year hiatus from reading, and I do this. I come back to one of the wretched Shadowhunter series. I was waiting to get my car fixed at Walmart a few days ago, and I decided to pick this book up. I don't know what I was expecting...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403452726ra/10095198.gif" width="180" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There are at least a few common things you can find in every Shadowhunter series.<br><br>1. Forbidden love or love triangle of some sort<br>2. Lots of angst but the bad kind<br>3. Long, awkward, and often cringe descriptions of make out sessions between love interests<br>4. Continuous descriptions of the main male protagonist's physical features and how they look in the sunlight or moonlight or whatever <br>5. Cheesy villain and his cliche backstory <br>6. Cardboard cutouts of past characters<br>7. Predictable <br><br>This book is nearly shit, obviously. I will explain the nearly later.<br><br>Firstly, why is this book so LONG!? Nearly 700 pages. It could have been much shorter if she cut out certain, unnecessary scenes. I suppose I forgot how long her books are. Hmm, must be the overly dramatic romance. Or the lengthy, cheesy descriptions of how everyone looks. For instance, what is this? I swear this is real. <br><br> <i>The sunlight illuminated his eyelashes.</i><br><br>I read something like that at the beginning of the book when she described Julian. I've always had a problem with Clare's writing but that just made me laugh out loud. That sentence should suffice. The rest of the book was just Clare describing how beautiful Julian looked at every hour of the day, or in every angle. This is the same thing that happened with Mortal Instruments. Jace and his golden eyes and caramel hair. Clary and her fiery red hair and emerald eyes. And this...<br><br><i>I was thinking about painting you. Painting your hair. That I'd have to use titanium white to get the color right, the way it catches light and almost glows. But that wouldn't work, would it? It's not all one color, your hair, it's not just gold: It's amber, and tawny and caramel and wheat and honey. </i><br><br>This is the most unrealistic shit I've ever come across. Men are absolute shit at seeing different colors. It's what they make fun of us women for! And Julian's seventeen. I get that he's a painter and all but STILL. I've seen this kind of crap way too many times for me to melt into a puddle of water.<br><br>Emma is disappointing. It's a shame that I hate most female protagonists, at least in YA books. I wish I had more positive experiences but man... She's annoying, childish, and arrogant. She isn't sassy or sarcastic or quick-witted as Clare intended her to be. She's just plain daft. Like, empty. She's basically Jace. And that immature shit she pulled at the end? I don't understand. She is just so contrived. <br><br>Julian is so bleh. He's the opposite of Jace, but he's not any better. He makes people feel bad that his life sucks, (he has to take care of kids and run a house -- therefore he deserves to be PRAISED AT ALL TIMES BOO HOO) is a painter (but paints literally only Emma... SHOCKING), wears a bracelet made of seashells or some shit, smells like cloves... why btw? I mean, JUST cloves is kind of gross. He's also very clingy. These kinds of romantic plots always irk me. I don't ever see the characters as themselves, just when they're together. <i>Always together.</i> So unbelievably together. Even when they're not together, they're together. Literally all Emma thinks of is Julian. All Julian ever thinks of is Emma. I mean, even with the whole parabatai stuff, is that really necessary? <br><br>Together, they are a disaster. Constantly whining about how they can't be together and how oh-so-painful it is. Haven't seen that before... Everyone is supposed to worship their perfect asses because they're the best Shadowhunters of their generation. Never seen that before either! Also, why do Emma and Julian need to HIDE their love in the first place? DOES ANYONE NOT SEE HOW ABSOLUTELY IN LURVE THEY ARE?! <br><br>The rest of the Blackthorn family are annoying. The only characters I enjoyed reading about were Mark and Christina. They are the least annoying, least contrived. Mark has a lot of dynamic. Christina is just so soft and pleasant and... quiet. She knows what to say and when to say it. I would love to read more about them in the next books. <br><br>I don't have much to say about the plot besides that it is so predictable and jaded. If Clare had not spent so much time describing how pretty and perfect and untouchable Emma and Julian were, maybe I would have paid more attention to it. Shame.<br><br>I'm not surprised. I'm not sure what I was expecting. All I know is that there is DEFINITELY something wrong with me. Because guess who'll be back to read and review the next installment of this beautiful series?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457985513ra/18429273.gif" width="185" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="14249772582539805012" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer577616007" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8700581698721618855"><b>DNF-ed at page. 337.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1515844353ra/24871885.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>(Link: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://giphy.com/gifs/the-gazette-uruha-WMuHoiZKQwSyI'>https://giphy.com/gifs/the-gazette-ur...</a>)<br/><br/>Rating: 1.5 stars.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1515683967ra/24867553.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>(Link: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://giphy.com/gifs/southparkgifs-3o6Zt8G9RsZpD1j76o'>https://giphy.com/gifs/southparkgifs-...</a>)<br/><br/>I admit this, I got fed up by Clare's constant Edgar Allan Poe references and when I skimmed to the ending part and saw <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Annabel Lee from Allan Poe's poem <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> being a mother fucking actual character in this book, I lost it and quit.<br/><br/>I am so pissed that I feel the need to write a 'poem' about this whole freaking Poe business:</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <br/>
  <br/> <b><u> Cassand</u></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText8700581698721618855" style="display:none"><b>DNF-ed at page. 337.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1515844353ra/24871885.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(Link: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://giphy.com/gifs/the-gazette-uruha-WMuHoiZKQwSyI">https://giphy.com/gifs/the-gazette-ur...</a>)<br><br>Rating: 1.5 stars.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1515683967ra/24867553.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(Link: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://giphy.com/gifs/southparkgifs-3o6Zt8G9RsZpD1j76o">https://giphy.com/gifs/southparkgifs-...</a>)<br><br>I admit this, I got fed up by Clare's constant Edgar Allan Poe references and when I skimmed to the ending part and saw <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Annabel Lee from Allan Poe's poem <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> being a mother fucking actual character in this book, I lost it and quit.<br><br>I am so pissed that I feel the need to write a 'poem' about this whole freaking Poe business:</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <br>
  <br> <b><u> Cassandra Clare</u></b><br><br><i>--a satire based *very* loosely on Annabel Lee, a poem by Edgar Allan Poe--</i><br><br>Author: Mizuki<br>Special Thank To: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/6431131-andre" rel="nofollow noopener">Andre</a><br>
  <br>
  <i>It was many many and many a year ago<br>In a kingdom of Badly Written YA Novels,<br>That an 'author' there lived who <br>By the name of Cassandra Clare<br>And this 'author' wrote novels<br>Filled with melodramas, Mary Sues and someone else's ideas<br><br>I was a reader and doomed to suffer,<br>In this kingdom of Badly Written YA,<br><br>For hardly anyone else could <br>Always fill her books with sheer meaninglessness,<br>The same like Cassandra Clare was capable of doing.<br><br>And this was the reason that, long ago<br>In this kingdom of Badly Written YA,<br>Cassandra Clare decided to fill her novels<br>With so many quotes,<br>Beautiful words taken from better authors and poets,<br>Cut out and stuffed into Clare's thick books.<br>Sadly these quotes serve no real purpose at all<br>In this kingdom of Badly Written YA.<br><br>I, the poor reader, not happy with Clare's awful use of,<br>Edger Allan Poe's quotes,<br>Is screaming in rage,<br>Yes! Why must The Conqueror Worm have anything, <br>To do with some guy turning into a worm,<br>In Clockwork Princess?<br><br>And why must Poe and Annabel Lee have<br>Any relation with demon hunters,<br>In the sunny Los Angeles?<br>Hell, it makes no sense.<br>Just like so many other contradictions<br>In Clare's Mortal Instruments Series.<br></i>
  <br>
</blockquote><br><b><br>In the very end, I hope you guys are as offended by my poor poem-writing-skill as I'm offended by Clare's stupid Poe's quotes.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1515683894ra/24867550.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(Link: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://giphy.com/gifs/southparkgifs-3o6ZtlOUjDE0RzCkX6">https://giphy.com/gifs/southparkgifs-...</a>)<br><br>Honestly, Clare's use of my idol Edgar Allan Poe as references isn't the biggest turn-off in this book yet, the real turn-off is the YA romance angst and how Clare wrote this book while fully expecting readers to care about the every little thing her characters do in their day-to-day lives and expecting readers to give a shit about these details.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1515683893ra/24867548.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(Link: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://giphy.com/gifs/edgar-allan-poe-zLRSQfRVDBwQ0">https://giphy.com/gifs/edgar-allan-po...</a>)<br><br>The problem is, characters need to be somewhat interesting for me to care about them, but Clare's characters, as usual, aren't even remotely interesting nor well constructed. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1515683893ra/24867549.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(Link: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://giphy.com/gifs/southparkgifs-l0HlKL0q92gfCDguQ">https://giphy.com/gifs/southparkgifs-...</a>)<br><br>Plus, at least 200 pages of this book could have been trimmed away, so where were Clare's editors when we need them the most?<br></b><br><br><u>
  <b>So, what had gone wrong? Here is a check list:</b>
</u><br><br><b>**Warning: slight plot spoilers below**</b><br><br><b>(1) The matter of simple mathematics</b><br><br>The population of L.A. : <b>3,976,322 (2016)</b><br><br>Number of Shadowhhunters: inclunding Emma, the Blackthorns, the Ashdowns, Diana and Cristina, etc; around 20-30 Shadow Hunters in total.<br><br>Number of demons: don't know, but supposedly there must be many demons in a large city like L.A.<br><br>So there are only 20 or so Shadowhunters to keep the demons in L.A. under control the whole time, it looks like the demons had been having plenty of slow days in L.A. all along.<br><br><b>(2) Uninteresting gay romances:</b><br><br>I always like gay/yaoi romances here and there, but OMG how can this certain someone think this faerie guy truly loves him because the faerie has been tender to him!?<br><br>Get real, please.<br><br><b>(3) The general stupidity of the Shadowhunters:</b> <br><br>First, these people allow Jace and Clary to run the New York Institute. *facepalms*<br><br>Secondly, when the wicked, manipulative faeries release a prisoner back to the L.A. Institute, our MCs do nothing to prevent said prisoner from harming the children. No, they haven't even suspected said prisoner might be brainwashed into harming them. No, they haven't even thought about this.<br><br>Thirdly, there seems to be no psychologist, no social worker, no orphans adoption system in the Shadowhunters society. <br><br>I mean, the adult Shadowhunters always died on missions and there had just been a massive war some five or six years ago, but in the Shadowhunters' society, we can still barely find one psychologist to help the survivors, no mention of PTSD treatment, no welfare system to look after the orphans.<br><br>Last but not least, no one outside of the L.A. Institute has ever realized their supposed chief is mentally ill and it is actually a few teenagers who are actually running things and fighting demons with little to no management from older Shadowhunters. <br><br><b>(4) I really don't like how Clare fully expects readers to be invested with her main characters when these characters have nothing to make me root for them:</b><br><br>Alright, I know I'm <i>supposed</i> to care about Emma and her investigation to find her parents' killer, I know I'm <i>supposed</i> to care about Julian, his emotional problems and his hotness, I know I'm also <i>supposed</i> to find the younger Blackthorn siblings cute and adorable---I'm <i>supposed</i> to care because that is exactly what Clare's tone and her writing has been indicating all along: most of the main characters were given a lengthy backstory, their daily routines (e.g. training, eating breakfast, throwing jokes at each other or simply chatting away, etc) are given the utmost attention and screen time; as though the daily routines and the internal monologues of these characters are so interesting that they all deserve readers' unlimited attention and time.<br><br><b>The truth is: they don't deserve that much of spaces and screen time.</b> I would rather see the plot moves forward in a bit of a faster pace instead of dealing with the Blackthorns siblings and their chatters, or the romantic angst between Emma and Julian, just to name a few of these annoyance. *sighs*<br><br><b>(5) When reading this book, I was trapped with some of the blandest and most boring main characters in my recent memory:</b><br><br>Let's face it, <b>Emma Carstairs and Julian Blackthorns are really <u>boring</u> both as a pair of BFF and potential love interest for each other.</b> One of the main problems is I just totally don't get Emma as a character, she seems to like fighting and training and wanting to avenge her parents.........and that's all I get from her as a character.<br><br>Not to mention, even when Emma is a supposedly well trained warrior, she still decides to carry a sword around 24/7 which makes no sense to me even when I know this sword is from her dead parents. She also tends to act purely out of impulse, randomly fighting demons and <b>going out to investigate demon activities without telling anyone where she is going---Stupid with a capital S damn it</b>, it is <b>just the same like Jace, all over again.</b><br><br>As to Julian, oh boy he is even more boring than Emma, although to be fair the guy has a bit more common sense and sense of responsibility in him than Emma, and as far as character's trait goes, he likes to paint and draw---still it just isn't enough to hook me with this character. I mean, am I really supposed to be invested with a character only because he is hot, he is into art and he has a sensitive soul? <br><br>To make matter worse, Clare wrote about Julian and his lengthy backstory fully expecting me to care about him as a person and his endless struggle with trying to raise 4 younger siblings since 12 or so years old. Okay, I know child-caring in such a young age is hard, still I feel nothing when I read about the hardship he faces.<br><br>I sense that with Julian and one of his younger brothers, Clare did try to address serious topics such as Special Education Needs and the problem of Shadowhunters not valuing their children's other talents (e.g. painting) outside of their fighting skills, but it just isn't enough to keep me interested; not even for 5 minutes.<br><br>As to the other Blackthorn siblings, <b>they are so freaking boring!</b> I understand that they are struggling to deal with the death of their father, the kidnapping of their older brother and the BS dished out to them by other adult Shadowhunters, but I simply can't guilt-trap myself into caring for any of them.<br><br>There also is Cristina...a Shadowhunter from Mexico! But as far as I can see, she is here only to show 'Look! There is a POC in the story!'<br><br><b>(6) the tiresome romantic woes between Emma and Julian take up a lot of spaces in the story: </b> <br><br>I have a feeling that Emma and Julian might not have turned out being so bland and uninteresting if all the romantic angst had been taken out from the storyline: they could have just been a case of "I like you, you like me, let's start dating!", or even better <b>they could have simply stayed friends for crying out loud.</b> That could have been kind of cute.<br><br>Instead, Clare decided these two need to have romantic angst, jealousy and misunderstanding between them, tons of it.<br><br>In order to get to the bottom of the unnecessary of the romantic woes between Emma and Julian, we must first get back to Point no. 3 in this review: the general stupidity of the Shadowhunters...especially the adults.<br><br>I mean all of the romantic angst between these two is established by the fact that they are parabatai---magic bound warrior partners with a bond which is supposedly unbreakable---and for some odd and unknown reason two parabatai aren't supposed to feel romantic love toward each other!<br><br>You think this taboo can keep Emma and Julian and their raging teenager's lust ridden hormones in check? You better think again!<br><br>So, <b>the whole point about Emma and Julian's feeling for each other being 'forbidden' is based solely on the foundation of them being parabatai;</b> and if you asked me, <b>this 'forbidden love' feels really forced and underwhelming to me,</b> even worse than the 'forbidden love' between Jace and Clary.<br><br>Plus it really makes zero sense to me when these adults just let Emma and Julian bind themselves to be parabatai at the tender age of 12, shortly after Emma suffered the trauma of losing both her parents. I mean, who in their right minds would allow two 12 years old kids making permanent life decision like this?!<br><br>To be honest, my good guess is by the end of the trilogy, Clare would find a loophole (no matter how far-fetched it is) for these two to break off their parabatai bond so they can sex each other up eventually.<br><br><b>(7) Nothing happens:</b><br><br>Last but not least, I'm getting to the most damaging part of this book's many flaws: <b>nothing happens in the first 300+ pages</b><br><br>We don't get much hint about the identity of the murderer of Emma's parents, we don't get much hint for the conspiracy surrounding the demon activities, for most of the time we don't even get much action scene. All we get is romantic subplots breeding left and right, and a lot of details about the daily activities of the Blackthorn family and their backstories.<br><br>300+ pages filled with these kind of nonsense is a bit too much for me. And trust me, if <i>Lady Midnight</i> doesn't have such kind of poor planning, shabby plots, awful pacing and nonexistent sense of direction, I wouldn't have DNF-ed it.<br><br><b>The Final Words:</b> don't buy it, don't borrow it, it just doesn't worth it.<br><br><u>Thoughts I have in the reading progress:</u><br><br>I am in the middle of this book and I wholeheartedly agree with this reviewer: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1907470299?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><br><u>Pre-review:</u><br><br>Another series within the poorly constructed world of Shadowhunters, a world which obviously is borrowed from Harry Potter?<br><br>Oh. My. Goodness.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380415792i/820949.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You know what I'm trying to say here, right?<br><br>I admit I'm being very negative here, but Cassandra Clare has so far given me almost nothing to be positive when it comes to her books.<br><br>And for those angry fans who say stuff like <i>"You shouldn't comment on a book you haven't yet read!"</i>, I want to share this comic (by Vicky/KurvosVicky), although his comic focuses on movies but the same can be well reflected on books and manga/comic<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1461733832i/18902763._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Original post: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://kurvosvicky.deviantart.com/art/Negative-Opinions-Not-Allowed-598462848">http://kurvosvicky.deviantart.com/art...</a><br><br>My review for <i>City <div id="review_294275736" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/294275736" />
    <a title="Carmen " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5879280-carmen"><img alt="Carmen " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1372641696p2/5879280.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/294275736?book_show_action=true">Mar 14, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carmen " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carmen " href="/user/show/5879280-carmen">Carmen </a>
      </span>

          marked it as to-read




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5879280-carmen?shelf=dying-to-read">dying-to-read</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer294275736" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7516975628325646359">WHY THE HELL IS everyone complaining that they think Cassie's writing more books to make cash?! True, I have my own complaints about never ending series, but when you have someone as talented as Cassie, IT KIND OF MAKES SENSE FOR HER TO WRITE MORE. Especially when many fans are ASKING FOR MORE. (ex. When everybody asked for more books in TMI series.) Honestly, I'm sure Cassie has other writing projects that she does that don't involve Shadowhunters, but I'm getting sick of biased people of judgi</span>
  <span id="freeText7516975628325646359" style="display:none">WHY THE HELL IS everyone complaining that they think Cassie's writing more books to make cash?! True, I have my own complaints about never ending series, but when you have someone as talented as Cassie, IT KIND OF MAKES SENSE FOR HER TO WRITE MORE. Especially when many fans are ASKING FOR MORE. (ex. When everybody asked for more books in TMI series.) Honestly, I'm sure Cassie has other writing projects that she does that don't involve Shadowhunters, but I'm getting sick of biased people of judging simply because this would be the third series of Shadowhunters that Cassie will be writing. (I don't see fans of Vampire Academy complaining that a spinoff series, Bloodlines is coming out. Or fans of Evermore, when Alyson Noel decided to write a series on Ever's sister.)<br />Why judge so harshly, read the book first. Who knows? It could end up being even better than TID AND TMI.<br /><br />***************<br /><br />Update: IT HAS A TITLE!!!! Lady Midnight!! YES.<br /><br />OMG OMG OMG OMG OMG OMG OMG<br /><br />YES!!!!!! <br /><br />I am highly anticipating for this book!!!! Cassandra Clare is one of my fav authors and I'm sure she will not disappoint! I can't wait to dive into a new Shadowhunter tale!<br /><br />*runs off screaming with joy, happiness, and frustration at why the book can't come out earlier*<br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
