<div id="review_2254629695" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2254629695" />
    <a title="amy ☂︎" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/61624004-amy"><img alt="amy ☂︎" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595924086p2/61624004.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2254629695?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="amy ☂︎" class="user" itemprop="url" name="amy ☂︎" href="/user/show/61624004-amy">amy ☂︎</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/61624004-amy?shelf=2018">2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/61624004-amy?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2254629695" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15040265820155540869">hoooooo boy. i don't really know where to start with this review, since i have so many mixed feelings regarding this book. but!!! not all of them are negative and i promise i have a lot of good things to say about the blackthorns so stay tuned everyone<br/><br/><u>
  <b>some positive and negative aspects:</b>
</u><br/><br/>let's get this out of the way. i went into this book expecting.... absolutely nothing. i'm not the biggest <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/150038.Cassandra_Clare' title='Cassandra Clare' rel='nofollow noopener'>cassandra clare</a> stan, and i could never see myself even remotely enjoying one of her books (yet, here </span>
  <span id="freeText15040265820155540869" style="display:none">hoooooo boy. i don't really know where to start with this review, since i have so many mixed feelings regarding this book. but!!! not all of them are negative and i promise i have a lot of good things to say about the blackthorns so stay tuned everyone<br><br><u>
  <b>some positive and negative aspects:</b>
</u><br><br>let's get this out of the way. i went into this book expecting.... absolutely nothing. i'm not the biggest <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/150038.Cassandra_Clare" title="Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">cassandra clare</a> stan, and i could never see myself even remotely enjoying one of her books (yet, here we are). i was convinced that the only good thing she ever created was <b>magnus bane</b> and that was it. i'm glad to say that i was wrong :-) don't get your hopes up yet, though, i will forever dislike the mortal instruments and i refuse to call myself a cc stan when i only enjoyed one (1) of her books. so much for the disclaimer<br><br>✔ <b>THE CHARACTERS</b><br>the characters really made this book for me. it would've been a way less enjoyable read for me if i hadn't learned to love the <b>blackthorn family</b> with my entire sinner heart. i'm going to go in depth later but for now, just know that i would die for each and every one of them. thank u<br><br>✖ <b>THE ROMANCE</b><br>i'm just not a big fan of the way cassie portrays romance, but then again, this might be a #me thing. i just.... don't..... like.... clichés.... and this is where you can't even argue with me, all the relationships she establishes between characters in her books are just soooooooooooooooooooooo CLICHÉ.<br><br><blockquote>
<u>exhibit a) ooooOOooOH nO! i'm falling in lOvE?!?! IMMEDIATE DENIAL!!!!</u><br><i>"[...]but he had luminous eyes and a beautiful mouth that-<br>She goggled at herself. What was <b>wrong</b> with her? What was wrong with her <b>thoughts</b>?"</i><br><br>spare me.<br><br><u>exhibit b) let's just make this moment here real dramatic and make them almost kiss but guess what, in the last second, thEY GET INTERRUPTED!!! genius</u><br><br>i'm tired. so tired. maybe i'm just too old to not be annoyed at the <b>typical ya tropes™</b> anymore<br><br><u>exhibit c) just..... no</u><br><br>the general cringe is just unavoidable in these books, i know, but if i have to read one more time how <i>person A wants to crawl inside person B's skin</i>, i'm going to throw the fuck up</blockquote><br><br>✔ <b>THE WRITING</b><br>you can really see that cassie improved her writing a lot from previous books. it's still not my favorite, but you can see an improvement.<br><br>✖ <b>THE PACING</b><br>who told cassie it was fine to a) make her chapters ten hours long and b) add the most unnecessary details?? i just wanna talk.<br>i remember being so bored throughout the entire book because everything was so <i>drawn-out</i> and <i>slow</i>; i felt actually exhausted at the thought of having to get through 600+ pages of it.<br><br>ok, i feel like that was enough ranting for now. onto the part where i scream for 3 hours over <b>how much i love the blackthorn family</b><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1516621773i/24898713._SY540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>♡<b>JULIAN BLACKTHORN</b><br>everyone deserves a mom like julian blackthorn tbh. i just *clenches fist* wish him all the best and hope he gets to be content and happy by the end of The Dark Artifices. this applies to most of the characters in this book, but if they get hurt i'm ready to fist fight <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/150038.Cassandra_Clare" title="Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">cassandra clare</a>. meet me in the pit bitch<br><br><i>
  <blockquote>"Julian determined that he would love them twice as fiercely as any adult could. He would do everything for them, he thought. [...] He would make sure they had everything they wanted. He would make sure they never missed what they didn't have; he would love them enough to make up for everything they'd lost."</blockquote>
</i> <br><br>name a better fictional mother than julian blackthorn. i'll wait<br><br>♡<b>EMMA CARSTAIRS</b><br>she was remarkably less annoying than clary, for sure. i still think all of cc's characters are somewhat trying to be hilarious and beautiful and perfect, but i didn't mind emma as much. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"You belong where you're loved."</i>
  <br>
  <br>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1516622911i/24898741._SY540_.jpg" width="242" height="360" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>♡<b>TIBERIUS BLACKTHORN</b><br>downright my favorite character in the entire book. he's so soft and weird and intelligent and my heart bursts for him!!! i love all the blackthorns but ty i would start wars and kill people for. not only that but...... i also <i>found myself</i> in him.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Ty had probably wandered off after an animal, was petting a squirrel or cuddling a stray cat. Or he might have shut himself away with a book, not wanting to socialize."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>ThatsMe.jpg<br><br>♡<b>MARK BLACKTHORN</b><br>know a fence but if you dislike mark take it up with me bitch!!! mark is a bisexual legend, an icon, a gentle soul that deserves nothing but joy and love. i rest my case<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1516623886i/24898751._SY540_.jpg" width="240" height="360" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>♡<b>THE BLACKTHORN FAMILY AS A WHOLE</b><br>listen, if i would talk about each and every one of them, this review would never end. i have Things to do.... People to meet..... no time for gushing about all these characters.<br><br>but i love dru and livvy and tavvy too, and i genuinely feel like they each added so much to this book. the blackthorns, to me, feel a little bit like the weasleys. you just can't help getting attached to every single one of them.<br><br>with that said, i hope cassie doesn't hurt them in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30312891.Lord_of_Shadows__The_Dark_Artifices___2_" title="Lord of Shadows (The Dark Artifices, #2) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">lord of shadows</a>. the thought of the blackthorns being safe and happy? #blessed #healed #content #glowing #complete<br><br><blockquote>❥<b>buddy read</b> with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/36873117-maram" rel="nofollow noopener">marami</a>
</blockquote></span>

Chain of Gold ★★★★★<br /><br />*.) The Bane Chronicles ★★★★<br />*.) Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy [TBA]<br />*.) Ghosts of the Shadow Market ★★★★<br /><br />-----------------------------------------------<br /><br />2018 - I still hate the ending so much.<br /><br />2016 - <br />Around The Year in 52 Books Challenge Notes:<br />52. A book that was published in 2016</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16152845381194303207"><i>JUST AS WONDERFUL AS THE FIRST TIME!!!</i> <br/><br/>The first time I read this, I read it in <b>one sitting</b> the night it was released. Yes, it was <b>that good</b>! All <i>700-ish</i> pages!!! <br/><br/>This time, I took <i>DAYS</i> to complete it because it’s the last month of uni. But that doesn’t mean it was any less <b>amazing</b>! <br/><br/><b>#Jemma</b> rivals some of my favourite ships in the Shadowhunter universe. Seriously, <b>Emma</b> is so badarse and <b>Julian</b> is so precious. They deserve <i>ALL THE HAPPINESS</i> in the world! <br/><br/>Also, <b>Mark</b> is hilarious. And the <b>Blackthorn</b></span>
  <span id="freeText16152845381194303207" style="display:none"><i>JUST AS WONDERFUL AS THE FIRST TIME!!!</i> <br /><br />The first time I read this, I read it in <b>one sitting</b> the night it was released. Yes, it was <b>that good</b>! All <i>700-ish</i> pages!!! <br /><br />This time, I took <i>DAYS</i> to complete it because it’s the last month of uni. But that doesn’t mean it was any less <b>amazing</b>! <br /><br /><b>#Jemma</b> rivals some of my favourite ships in the Shadowhunter universe. Seriously, <b>Emma</b> is so badarse and <b>Julian</b> is so precious. They deserve <i>ALL THE HAPPINESS</i> in the world! <br /><br />Also, <b>Mark</b> is hilarious. And the <b>Blackthorn siblings</b> were just too cute. I absolutely love this world (I believe this is the 13th Shadowhunter book I've read???) and the characters within it, including the <i>cameos</i> from the other series!!! <br /><br />I’m going out of town though, so I’ll review it when I return. <b>RTC</b>!</span>

<div id="review_2448870803" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2448870803" />
    <a title="Fares" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/58818027-fares"><img alt="Fares" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581798339p2/58818027.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2448870803?book_show_action=true">Jul 07, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Fares" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Fares" href="/user/show/58818027-fares">Fares</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58818027-fares?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2448870803" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3837506214652427737">Everyone knows that 4 is the perfect amount of reads, so don't judge me. Or was it 5? Maybe just to be sure I'll reread for the fifth time sometime :)<br/>-------------------------------<br/>Now I want to watch Notting Hill 😂<br/>-------------------------------<br/><b>I…</b><br/><i>*Breaths in*</i><br/><b>don’t…</b><br/><i>*Breaths out*</i><br/><b>know…</b><br/><i>*Breaths in*</i><br/><b>what’s…</b><br/><i>*Breaths out*</i><br/><b>happening…</b><br/><i>*Breaths in*</i><br/><br/>Why am I so emotionally drained?<br/>Why am I so emotionally invested in these characters?<br/>Why do I feel so sad that they do not exist? And why do I want to cry because</span>
  <span id="freeText3837506214652427737" style="display:none">Everyone knows that 4 is the perfect amount of reads, so don't judge me. Or was it 5? Maybe just to be sure I'll reread for the fifth time sometime :)<br />-------------------------------<br />Now I want to watch Notting Hill 😂<br />-------------------------------<br /><b>I…</b><br /><i>*Breaths in*</i><br /><b>don’t…</b><br /><i>*Breaths out*</i><br /><b>know…</b><br /><i>*Breaths in*</i><br /><b>what’s…</b><br /><i>*Breaths out*</i><br /><b>happening…</b><br /><i>*Breaths in*</i><br /><br />Why am I so emotionally drained?<br />Why am I so emotionally invested in these characters?<br />Why do I feel so sad that they do not exist? And why do I want to cry because of that? And why had I cried because of that? And why, just <b>why do they not exist?</b><br /><br />I don’t know what’s happening to me ☹ I really don't know and so I’m going to reread just one day after I finished.<br />---<br />The reread is done and I understand more and less at the same time.<br /><br />It’s so confusing that I love this book and there are things I don’t want to love, things that honestly I’m kind of scared to be liking, things like the love triangle and the “lowkey” cheating. There’s always some of that in Cassandra’s books and it’s something that always bothered me but not in this book, I don’t think I’d go as far as saying I enjoyed them but I didn’t mind them as much as I did before, I loved the characters too much to hate them for that, <b>Is that a bad thing? That I love these characters so much I’m ready to ignore something I believe to be wrong.</b><br /><br />The other thing is the romance, this may not be as big of an issue as the love triangle and the cheating, maybe some of you will see it as no issue at all, but for someone like me who always saw it as a secondary thing, the plot first romance second, it’s weird to fall for this book, it is weird to daydream about it and it is weird to feel so much… *sigh*.<br /><br />I never mind the romance, I enjoy it but I don’t see it as the driving force for a book, or at least I thought so, now I’m not sure. I used to skip such scenes, blushing and mortified that maybe someone noticed what I just read even when I completely alone 😂. And now after reading this and rereading it, I love it? I’m not sure, as I said I’m so confused. I’m not saying it’s not okay to love it, I just don’t understand why this book of all made me feel this way? Why do I… *sigh again*<br /><br />There’s a knot over my chest and I don’t know how to get rid of it and I think I’m slumping.<br /><br />I don’t think this is the kind of reviews you guys signed up for, I’m sorry I’m not sure how to go on about it honestly.<br /><br />I think there are 3 questions that need answering about this book for you to know my experience reading this book and I’ll try and answer them.<br /><b>What did you love about this book?<br />What did you hate about this book?<br />What did you find unique about this book?</b><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>What do you love about this book?</b>
</blockquote>Two characters. While I do love all the character in various degrees, these two are love and joy and life, they are heartbreak and tears and death. They are my heart.<br /><br /><b>Octavian Blackthorn</b><br /><br /><i>“Tavvy was standing by a whiteboard with a blue dry-erase marker, making possibly helpful notations, if they could ever be translated out of seven-year-old.”</i><br /><br />You can’t hate Tavvy, you just can’t.<br />There are no words in this world to tell you how I feel about him, at least not words that I know of. This is terrible because I want to say so much about him but I don’t know how, so here are almost all of Tavvy’s scenes in the book, there are no spoilers but I tagged them just in case you wanted to know him reading the book.<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />-<i>The room contained a small bed with a brightly striped coverlet, a playhouse nearly as tall as Emma, and a tent full of books and toys. “Tavvy has nightmares,” Emma said. “Sometimes Julian comes and sleeps in the tent with him.”</i><br /><br />-<i>Beside them was Drusilla, holding the hand of the youngest, Tavvy. He looked asleep on his feet, his curly head against Dru’s arm, his eyes closed.</i><br /><br />-<i>“Dru told me that faeries steal your teeth while you’re sleeping,” Tavvy said.</i><br /><br />-<i> Tavvy had woken up and was wandering around sleepily, tugging on people’s sleeves. Emma ruffled his hair.</i><br /><br />-<i>Tavvy had curled up on the floor and was asleep in the angled beam of light from a lamp, exactly like a cat.</i><br /><br />-<i>“Tavvy!” Julian said. “Don’t run with lollipops in your mouth. You could choke.”<br />Tavvy removed the lollipop and stared at it the way someone might stare at a loaded gun. “And die?”<br />“Hideously,” Julian said. “Fatally, fatally die.”</i><br /><br />-<i>“How many have died, exactly? People and faeries?”<br />“Twelve,” said Emma. “Twelve dead bodies.”<br />Tavvy emerged from under the table. “Were they all running with lollipops?”</i><br /><br />-<i>Tavvy was standing by a whiteboard with a blue dry-erase marker, making possibly helpful notations, if they could ever be translated out of seven-year-old.</i><br /><br />-<i>“Oso.” Tavvy took the bear and smiled a gap-toothed smile</i><br /><br />-<i>Tavvy was a curled-up ball under the covers of his bed. He was asleep, his body curved around one of his pillows, his mouth open on a gasp. Tears ran down his face.</i><br /><br />-<i>A massive bag of powdered sugar had been torn open and Tavvy was sitting inside it, completely covered in white powder. He looked like a tiny abominable snowman.</i><br /><br />-<i>Julian felt a pang for his smallest brother, so often trapped in rooms full of older people talking about blood and death.</i><br /><br />-<i>“Because it’s a children’s book,” said Emma. “It wouldn’t have been in the library.”<br />“That’s dumb,” said Tavvy serenely. “It’s a good book.”</i><br /><br />-<i>Livvy gave a little gasp, reaching for the book. Hesitantly, Tavvy let her have it.<br />“Don’t tear the pages,” he warned.</i><br /><br />-<i>All she could see was Tavvy, little Tavvy, the smallest Blackthorn. Tavvy having nightmares, Tavvy in her arms as she carried him through the war-torn Institute five years ago. Tavvy covered in paint in Jules’s studio. Tavvy, who alone among them had skin that could not hold a single protection rune. Tavvy, who would not understand what was happening to him or why.</i><br /><br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Julian Blackthorn</b><br />Every time his uncle calls him Andrew my heart shatters.<br /><br />I have a place I go to, a special place, it’s not a secret or a hidden place but I think of it as my place, I go to it when I need to think, when I need to make sense of things, I go to it almost every day, not because I need to make sense of things every day but because it’s a common place, it only becomes special when I need it to be. I guess it’s not a special place exactly but a place for special things, it’s a place only made special by me and the thoughts I have while I’m in there.<br /><br />I shared my place with only two book characters, only two characters made me want to spend an afternoon, just me alone with my thoughts, just me alone with them, thinking.<br />Only two book characters made me love them so much I hated them for being fictional.<br />Julian Blackthorn is one of them.<br /><br />Julian is whom I wish to be, I relate to him in some ways and that was more than enough for me. I want him to be happy, I want him to be hugged and be told that he’s loved, I want him to see himself as I see him. He makes me want to be better, he cares for his family, he’ll do anything for them and expects nothing in return.<br />Julian is the guardian angel for the people he loves, and his love for them makes him go out of his way, he’ll do wrong things to keep this family together and you can tell he hates it because he’s just the purest soul.<br /><br />I don’t know if I’m lucky or not, if you ever felt what I’m feeling you know what I’m talking about. <b>Have you ever loved a character so much, in one hand you’re happy that you know them and in the other hand what does your life mean if you can’t protect them? if you can only wait to see what happens to them and you can’t do anything about it, what's the point if you're going to be absolutely helpless?</b><br /><br />Maybe I’m just being overdramatic and I won’t feel the same tomorrow but I don’t want to read anything now, not that I can anyway.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>What did you hate about this book?</b>
</blockquote><b>Mark</b><br /><br />Okay so this is what I wrote about Mark while I was reading, it’s unedited and I should say that Mark made me feel more confusion than hate, I think this shows as you read these unedited notes.<br /><br />Mark is what I hate about this book he’s generally what I hate about most of Casandra Clare’s books.<br />He is all over the place with his feelings and I hate it when a character’s feelings for another comes before his family and unfortunately that is Mark.<br /><br />I feel sorry for what he has been through but he blames Julian for not trying to find him <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[while he himself is having thoughts of leaving them <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, Julian was 12. And no one, NO ONE has the right to say anything to Julian.<br /><br /><i>“He seemed like someone who had woken up after a hundred years of sleep, shaking the dust of a century’s dreams from his feet. He had been terrified...”</i><br /><br />Mark has suffered, he’s hurt body and soul and I hate what happened to him, he makes me so confused, I don’t want to hate him but.<br />Granted this is not a perfect situation but everyone seems to be trying except him.<br /><br /><i>“I am Julian’s parabatai,” she said. “And Julian needs you to stay.”<br />“Julian is strong,” he said.<br />“Julian is strong,” she agreed. “But you are his brother. And if you go—I don’t know if I can pick up those pieces.”<br />His eyes flicked back to her closet. “We survive losses,” he whispered.</i> <br /><br />We do survive but that doesn’t mean we should inflict them voluntarily on the ones we love, and Julian already lost way too much, why is he the only one that needs to survive the losses while everyone else finds their escape.<br /><br /><b>Where the plot is going.</b><br /><br />This is more of a guess but the way I’m seeing the story is going is not something I like then again what do I know, I thought I won’t like this and look at me now.<br />The way I see the story is Julian having to make hard choices between Emma and his family, I don’t like that, it’s what I hate about most characters, that they sacrifice their family for the one they love, not only do I hate it but also I don’t see Julian doing that and if he does I’d be so disappointed, it’ll make all the feels he had for his siblings seem fake and that will break my heart.<br /><br />And the love shapes, I always hate those and it seems there are going to be more of those.<br /><br /><b>I have to say though that both of those problems didn’t bother me much as I fell head over heels for the characters.<br />Also I think I hated perfect Diego but I haven’t seen much of him to be sure.<br /><br />Also why is there no female characters like Julian or Jem from TID? I always like the male characters in these books more, if there was a female Julian, my life would be perfect.</b><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>What did you find unique about this book?</b>
</blockquote> Unique doesn’t necessarily mean good.<br /><br />This book took me by surprise, I didn’t expect at all to fall in love with it this much probably because of the previous experiences with Shadowhunters, so my expectations weren’t high but to feel this much for a book you thought so little of, it’s overwhelming.<br /><br /><b>How I didn’t mind the plot</b><br /><br />Let me be honest for a second here, Cassandra Clare’s book are less about the fantasy element and more about YA and that’s not a bad thing except that I always go into them with a fantasy mindset, that makes me focus on the plot and less about the other things and when the plot becomes predictable I lose interest but that didn’t happen with this one, this book actually restored my faith in contemporaries, recently I wasn’t in the mood for them but now I want them more and I love it more for that.<br /><br />I just love some characters beyond what I thought possible, that made me ignore a lot of things just the happiness of my beloved characters, that’s all I wanted.<br /><br /><b>How I loved the romance.</b><br /><br />As I said in the beginning, I love the romance in this book, I don’t know how to approach this and I'm blushing just thinking about it so umm I'll leave it at that.<br /><br /><b>How much I cried</b><br /><br />It’s not that much but it happened more than I expected and this isn’t the most heartbreaking book ever. I don’t know why exactly this happened and I asked myself that so many times, at one point I believed something is wrong with me.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>Other things</b>
</blockquote>Here are things that added to the entire experience.<br /><br /><b>Emma</b><br /><br />Emma is ruthless, she doesn’t go in roundabout ways, she’s a straightforward rip off the band-aid kind of girl.<br /><br /><i>“Half the scars Emma had on her body she’d put there herself, teaching herself to fall from the highest rafters, training herself to fight through pain by practicing barefoot—on broken glass.”</i><br /><br /><i>“This is about me, not you,” she said into the phone. Cristina gave her an encouraging thumbs-up. “I am sick of you.” She smiled brightly as Cristina dropped her face into her hands. “So maybe we could go back to being friends?”<br />There was a click as he hung up.</i> <br /><br />That was funny, I laughed at that until Christina pointed out that in two months Emma forgot three dates with him, skipped his birthday and dumped him because it was a slow patrol night.<br />This what makes me conflicted about her, she’s strong and can do what others can’t but she can be cruel and harsh too.<br /><br />She loves her best friend Cristina.<br /><br />She’s rebellious and hates some of the laws the Clave made and when those laws stand on her way to discover what happened to her parents she doesn’t hesitate to break them. That makes me excited to see what she’ll do when the laws stand between her and love.<br /><br /><b>Cristina</b><br /><br />She has a past and she’s trying to forget it.<br /><br />As Emma said about her <i>“… she’d always had the air of someone running from something.”</i><br /><br />She loves Emma, I think they even could’ve been parabatai if Emma wasn’t with Julian.<br /><br /><i>She brushed her hands through Emma’s hair, looking at her worriedly. “You sure you’re not hurt?”<br />“Julian’s blood,” Emma whispered, and Cristina made a murmuring noise and pulled Emma into a hug. She patted Emma’s back and Emma hung on to her for dear life and decided there and then that if anyone ever tried to hurt Cristina she would grind them to a pulp and make amusing sand castles out of the remains.</i><br /><br /><b>Dru</b><br /><br /><i>“Dru loves horror movies,” said Emma. “Anything with the word ‘blood’ or ‘terror’ or ‘prom’ in it.</i><br /><br />Dru of all the Blackthorns I want to befriend, they all have someone that can be considered their other half except for her and that’s unacceptable because she’s the best, THE BEST.<br /><br /><b>Livvy</b><br /><br /><i>“Books about computers and programming languages were stacked in careful rows by her bed.”</i><br /><br />I thought of Kady from Illuminae right after I read that. Livvy is my girl I just wish we had more of her, I think she would’ve been my favorite.<br /><br /><b>Ty</b><br /><br /><i>“On the bedside table were his most beloved books: Arthur Conan Doyle’s Sherlock Holmes stories.”</i><br /><br />I think Ty is a combination of me and my sister, and I can’t not love him. He and Livvy both have a half of my heart, they are both so precious.<br /><br /><i>“Livvy, who knew better than anyone the anxiety that imprecise language could cause her brother, scrambled to her feet and went over to him. She put her arms around him, her chin against his shoulder. Ty leaned against her, his eyes half-lidded...”</i><br /><br /><b>The writing</b><br /><br />The writing was beautiful, there are moments when I stopped reading and just closed my eyes and started dreaming. That’s not always the case though, I found that some parts of the book are better written than others.<br />That is not to say that it was bad, just some part like the prologue and such were more beautiful than others. Maybe this is just me and how I swoon over descriptive writing (if it doesn’t drag for long which it didn’t) I think what I’m trying to say is the writing was okay with some beautiful moments <br /><br />This is all I have, I'm actually tired 😂 and this was embarrassing.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>The End.</i>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="3837506214652427737" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText3948630645266096135" style="display:none">Let me guess: this "Julian" fellow is going to be snarky and sarcastic just like every other love interest CC has written about. <br /><br />I mean, really, where do they get it from? <br /><br />Sure, I LOVE when the main guy in a story is sarcastic and witty, but seriously...try something new. <br /><br />And just by experience, I can already predict things that are going to happen: <br /><br />1) There is going to be another love triangle in which I can predict the ending FROM the first sentence. <br /><br />2) CC is going to over-use certain adjectives explaining Julian's eyes/hair/body, etc. <br /><br />3) They'll end up together.     <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1358375395" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1358375395" />
    <a title="Simona B" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5312173-simona-b"><img alt="Simona B" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1408893128p2/5312173.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1358375395?book_show_action=true">Aug 08, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Simona B" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Simona B" href="/user/show/5312173-simona-b">Simona B</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781471116612" href="/book/show/24851136-lady-midnight">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5312173-simona-b?shelf=fantastic-lit-and-co">fantastic-lit-and-co</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5312173-simona-b?shelf=in-english">in-english</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5312173-simona-b?shelf=2000">2000</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1358375395" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8118937646779298571"><b>EDIT</b> 11/04/2016: I had rounded up my rating to four stars, but now I don't remember why on earth I did it. The book pretty much left me nothing. Which is sad, I know. So I'm lowering the rating to three stars.<br/><br/><b>"It hurt me being away from you. It feels like there’s a hook dug under my ribs, and there’s something pulling at the other end. Like I’m tethered to you, no matter the distance."</b><br/><br/>Beware the Jane Eyre references, people.<br/><br/>Let it be clear: I am a sucker for <b>best-friends-falling-in-love stories</b>.</span>
  <span id="freeText8118937646779298571" style="display:none"><b>EDIT</b> 11/04/2016: I had rounded up my rating to four stars, but now I don't remember why on earth I did it. The book pretty much left me nothing. Which is sad, I know. So I'm lowering the rating to three stars.<br /><br /><b>"It hurt me being away from you. It feels like there’s a hook dug under my ribs, and there’s something pulling at the other end. Like I’m tethered to you, no matter the distance."</b><br /><br />Beware the Jane Eyre references, people.<br /><br />Let it be clear: I am a sucker for <b>best-friends-falling-in-love stories</b>. Even if they are averagely written, paired with an average plot, featuring mediocre characters (please note that I am not saying this is <i>Lady Midnight</i>’s case), I’m very likely to enjoy them. Not enough to give them a high rating, probably, simply because that’s not how I rate, but to enjoy, even mildly, yes. Long story short: I enjoyed <i>Lady Midnight</i>. There is a bunch of things about this book that I found rather bothersome, but, all in all, <b>I enjoyed it</b> sounds like a fair and encompassing enough way to put it.<br /><br />•The <b>plot</b> is good, surely more than I expected and more than what I remembered Clare was capable of. It positively surprised me, and that’s definitely a selling point. <b>Fast-paced</b> (though the first part was a little too slow) without losing focus on the characters, <b>action-packed</b> without giving off the impression of being messy or crammed, and in this it is very <b>well-balanced</b>. I still think, though, that the book is too long. It didn’t exactly bore me, but at one point I just wanted it to end. And the ending is clearly drawn-out. It could have been packed up more nicely, in my opinion. <br /><br />•In the first part there are two or three clumsy and <b>awkward infodump</b>. And<b> I understand</b> that the book is supposed to be suitable even for those readers who have no idea of what happened before, but there are elegant explanations and then there are cumbersome infodumps. <br /><br />•I really, sincerely like the Blackthorns, which is quite astonishing because Cassie never managed to make me care so deeply for her characters -except for Magnus and Alec, but even there, I don’t care exactly for <i>them</i>, but rather for their relationship.<b> Julian Blackthorn</b> is probably my favorite character among all of those Clare ever created: he has this peculiar blend of tenderness and harshness inside of him (he does a pretty cruel thing at the end of the book that totally won me over, and the way he tends to and cares for his siblings is incredibly heart-warming), and <b>controversial characters</b> always find their way to my heart. In my mind, I picture him as a cute killer panda. Yeah, cute killer panda it is.<br />One thing that Clare could really spare us? His tirade about true love. That was silly, dumb and embarrassing. The only missing thing were a couple of squirrels and rabbits to sing along, Snow White style.<br /><br />•Emma. <i>Emma</i>. Please. <br />I knew Clare pretty clearly sucks at creating likeable female heroines, but this is the third failure out of three. <b>That takes talent</b>.<br />So, people, meet<b> Emma Carstairs</b>: <b>hot-headed</b>, <b>foolhardy</b>, <b>stubborn</b>, in short, everything I don’t associate with an admirable heroine. As if that were not enough, she managed to further destroy the ending by adopting the <b>infamous</b>, <b>ignoble</b>, <b>hateful</b>, <b>unbecoming</b> (no kidding, I really loathe this device) <b>silent strategy</b>.<br />No.<br /><i>No</i>.<br />I hate this thing with my entire being.<br />It never works! Authors, authors, when will you come to the conclusion that it’s a stupid, unnerving and immature thing to make your characters do and that you -at least, some of you- can do better than that? <i>When</i>?!<br /><br />*inhales deeply*<br /><br />Ok. Ok, I am calm now. But we really didn't need all that <b>useless drama</b> nor all the drama that will necessarily follow in the next books.<br /><br />So, as you have gathered, I despised Emma most of the time. <i>But</i> I deeply, profoundly adored what she did <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[for Julian when Iarlath was whipping him. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. That scene is my favorite in the whole book and probably in all the Shadowhunters series.<b> Marvellous</b>. Just marvellous.<br /><br />•The <b>romance</b>- was it only an impression of mine, or the whole thing felt very <b>anticlimactic</b>? I don’t know, I expected much more tension which at the end of the day wasn’t delivered. But I wouldn’t be surprised if it was just me because, remember, I’m a sucker for this kind of stories and so on. I probably expected the moon. So take this with a grain of salt.<br /><br />•I don’t ship Mark and Cristina -I actually think she’s better off with Diego. That probably didn’t require a paragraph of his own, but I didn’t know where to put it.<br /><br /><u>In a nutshell</u>: it was a full four-star rating until that unnecessary dramatic ending, so <b>I recommend the book</b>, and I think that the fans of the Shadowhunters world will be more than satisfied with it –a lot of references and cameos, speaking about this. I will need some time to shake the irritation off me (that ridiculous ending! Argh!) but, all things considered, I had a good time. <br /><br />(And Julian is <i>so</i> cute you can’t really be angry with this book, so…)<br /><br /><b>PRE-READING</b>: 'kay, Cassie, let's see if you can make me fall in love this time around. Don't they say the third series's the charm?<br /><br /><b>EDIT</b> 9/10/2015: Please tell me I am not the only one already shipping Emma and Jules like crazy when the book is not even out yet. <br />Hello, normality.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8118937646779298571" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('tpxfGWr8Oi7ad1dQY8devWQqNN3WbRToooFc63+i02s9Za8VkWgG1jD1JsC2dSmwmqOxl0LlUod5mABPO9K1Nw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('gME6yHJc2JoxPQbl25ZNZRQixmkGBI0Z723xKcQcZT0LOMrEicjkYtu/d3UOJDpo6qtDI5KMy3Y0dK2NgGwDYQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

But Elfhame is not as she left it. War is brewing. <span id="freeTextContainer14623949315516001977">Hello Goodreadsers. Here's my official bio:<br/><br/>"Cassandra Clare was born overseas and spent her early years traveling around the world with her family and several trunks of fantasy books. Cassandra worked for several years as an entertainment journalist for the Hollywood Reporter before turning her attention to fiction. She is the author of City of Bones, the first book in the Mortal Instruments trilo</span>
  <span id="freeText14623949315516001977" style="display:none">Hello Goodreadsers. Here's my official bio:<br /><br />"Cassandra Clare was born overseas and spent her early years traveling around the world with her family and several trunks of fantasy books. Cassandra worked for several years as an entertainment journalist for the Hollywood Reporter before turning her attention to fiction. She is the author of City of Bones, the first book in the Mortal Instruments trilogy and a New York Times bestseller. Cassandra lives with her fiance and their two cats in Massachusetts."<br /><br />You can find me online at <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.cassandraclare.com">www.cassandraclare.com</a><br /><br />I have a blog:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://cassandraclare.livejournal.com/">http://cassandraclare.livejournal.com/</a><br /><br />and a Facebook:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/Cassandraclare">http://www.facebook.com/Cassandraclare</a><br /><br />and a Twitter:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.twitter.com/cassieclare">www.twitter.com/cassieclare</a><br /><br />I'll be available here on Goodreads to answer questions for a Goodreads Author Discussion starting September 18 — <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/37113.Q_A_with_Cassandra_Clare">http://www.goodreads.com/group/show/3...</a><br /><br />Go sign up so you don't miss the conversation when it starts!</span>

You know their dreams because their nightmares pierce your heart and their good dreams are your dreams too. And you don't think they're perfect, but you know their flaws, the deep-down truth of them, and the shadows of all their secrets, and they don't frighten you away; in fact you love them more for it, because you don't want perfect.
